Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - State System of Higher Education
==================================================================

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 1 - Governance, Powers, Rights, and Responsibilities
**********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this title:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1)(a): "Academic education" means an educational program that is offered by a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1)(b): "Academic education" does not include technical education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(2): 53B-1-402 "Board" means the Utah Board of Higher Education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3): "Career and technical education" means an educational program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(a): is designed to meet industry needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b): leads to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b)(i): a certificate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b)(ii): a degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(c): may qualify for funding under the Carl D. Perkins Career and Technical Education Improvement Act of 2006, 20 U.S.C. 2301 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(4): 53B-1-408 "Commissioner" means the commissioner of higher education appointed in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(5): 53B-1-102(1)(a) "Degree-granting institution of higher education" or "degree-granting institution" means an institution of higher education described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6): 53B-2-103; 53B-2a-108 "Institution board of trustees" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6)(a): 53B-2-103 an institution of higher education board of trustees described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6)(b): 53B-2a-108 a technical college board of trustees described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(7): 53B-1-102(1)(b) "Technical college" means an institution of higher education described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a): "Technical education" means career and technical education that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a)(i): leads to a certificate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a)(ii): is short-term training.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(b): "Technical education" does not include general education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.8 Health insurance mandates.
------------------------------------------------------------
An institution of higher education shall include in a health plan it offers to its employees insurance mandates in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102 Utah system of higher education.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1): The Utah system of higher education consists of the following institutions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a): degree-granting institutions, which are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(i): the University of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(ii): Utah State University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(iii): Weber State University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(iv): Southern Utah University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(v): Snow College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(vi): Utah Tech University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(vii): Utah Valley University; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(viii): Salt Lake Community College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b): technical colleges, which are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(i): Bridgerland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(ii): Davis Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(iii): Dixie Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(iv): Mountainland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(v): Ogden-Weber Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(vi): Southwest Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(vii): Tooele Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(viii): Uintah Basin Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(c): the Utah Board of Higher Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(d): other public post-high school educational institutions as the Legislature may designate.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(2): A change in the name of an institution within the Utah system of higher education is not a change in the role or mission of the institution, unless otherwise authorized by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(3): It is not the intent of the Legislature to increase the number of research universities in the state beyond the University of Utah and Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(4): (1) An institution or board described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-108 Board succeeds to rights and duties of predecessor board and council.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board is the successor to and is vested with all rights, duties, obligations, and liabilities to which its predecessor governing boards and the Coordinating Council of Higher Education were subject, except as otherwise provided by law.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109 Coordination of higher education and public education information technology systems -- Use of unique student identifier.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1): 53B-33-201; 53B-1-102; 53E-4-308 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(a): 53B-33-201 "Center" means the Utah Data Research Center created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(c): 53E-4-308 "Unique student identifier" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2): 53E-4-308 The board and State Board of Education, in collaboration with the center, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2)(a): 53E-4-308 coordinate public education and higher education information technology systems to allow individual student academic achievement to be tracked through both education systems in accordance with this section and Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2)(b): coordinate access to the unique student identifier of a public education student who later attends an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(3): Information technology systems used at an institution of higher education shall use the unique student identifier of all students who have previously been assigned a unique student identifier.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110 Criminal background checks of prospective and existing employees of higher education institutions -- Board to adopt policy.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1)(a): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1)(b): "Minor" means a person younger than 21 years of age.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2): The board shall adopt a policy providing for criminal background checks of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2)(a): prospective employees of institutions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2)(b): existing employees of institutions, where reasonable cause exists.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3): (3)(a)(i); (3)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a): The policy shall require that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a)(i): an applicant for any position that involves significant contact with minors or any position considered to be security sensitive by the board or its designee shall submit to a criminal background check as a condition of employment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a)(ii): an existing employee submit to a criminal background check, where reasonable cause exists.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(b): (3)(a)(i) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(c): (3)(a)(i) The policy may allow or require applicants for positions other than those described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(d): The policy may allow criminal background checks for new employees to be phased in over a two-year period.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(4): The applicant or employee shall receive written notice that the background check has been requested.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5): Each applicant or employee subject to a criminal background check under this section shall, if required by the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(a): be fingerprinted; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b): consent to a fingerprint background check by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b)(i): the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b)(ii): the Federal Bureau of Investigation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6): (7)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(a): Institutions may request the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification to conduct criminal background checks of prospective employees and, where reasonable cause exists, existing employees pursuant to board policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b): At the request of an institution, the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b)(i): release the individual's full record of criminal convictions to the administrator requesting the information; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b)(ii): seek additional information from regional or national criminal data files in responding to inquiries under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(c): Information received by the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification from entities other than agencies or political subdivisions of the state may not be released to a private entity unless the release is permissible under applicable laws or regulations of the entity providing the information.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(d): (7) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(7): The board may by policy require an applicant to pay the costs of a criminal background check as a condition of employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(8): The applicant or employee shall have an opportunity to respond to any information received as a result of the criminal background check.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(9): If a person is denied employment or is dismissed from employment because of information obtained through a criminal background check, the person shall receive written notice of the reasons for denial or dismissal and have an opportunity to respond to the reasons under procedures established by the board in policy.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112 Disclosure requirements for institution programs.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1): 53B-1-102; (1)(e)(i)(A); (B); (C) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(a): "Department" means the Department of Workforce Services.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(c): "Job placement data" means information collected by the board, and based on information from the department, that reflects the job placement rate and industry employment information for a student who graduates from a program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i): "Program" means a program of organized instruction or study at an institution that leads to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(A): an academic degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(B): a professional degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(C): a vocational degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(D): a certificate of one year or greater or the direct assessment equivalent; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(E): another recognized educational credential.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(ii): "Program" includes instruction or study that, in lieu of time as a measurement for student learning, utilizes direct assessment of student learning, or recognizes the direct assessment of student learning by others, if the assessment is consistent with the accreditation of the institution or program utilizing the results of the assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e): (1)(e)(i)(A); (B); (C) "Student loan information" means the percentage of students at an institution who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i): received a Title IV loan authorized under:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(A): the Federal Perkins Loan Program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(B): the Federal Family Education Loan Program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(C): the William D. Ford Direct Loan Program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(ii): (1)(e)(i)(A); (B); (C) fail to pay a loan described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f): "Total costs" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i): the estimated costs a student would incur while completing a program, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i)(A): tuition and fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i)(B): books, supplies, and equipment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii): calculated based on a student's degree, the institution's average costs that would be incurred while a student completes a program and are subsidized by taxpayer contribution, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii)(A): tuition and fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii)(B): other applicable expenses subsidized by taxpayer contribution for program completion.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(g): "Wage data" means information collected by the board, and based on information from the department, that reflects a student's wage the first year and fifth year after a student has successfully completed a program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2): (4); (2)(b); (3); (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a): (4); (2)(b); (3) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a)(i): job placement data;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113 Education loan notifications.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a): "Borrower" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a)(i): an individual enrolled in an eligible postsecondary institution who receives an education loan; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a)(ii): an individual, including a parent or legal guardian, who receives an education loan to fund education expenses of an individual enrolled in an eligible postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b): "Education loan" means a loan made to a borrower that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b)(i): made directly by a federal or state program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b)(ii): insured or guaranteed under a federal or state program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c): "Eligible postsecondary institution" means a public or private postsecondary institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c)(i): is located in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c)(ii): participates in federal student assistance programs under the Higher Education Act of 1965, Title IV, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1070 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2): Annually, on or before July 1, an eligible postsecondary institution that receives information about a borrower's education loan shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(a): notify the borrower that the borrower has an education loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(b): direct the borrower to the National Student Loan Data System described in 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1092b to receive information about the borrower's education loan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(c): provide the borrower information on how the borrower can access an online repayment calculator.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(3): An eligible postsecondary institution does not incur liability for information provided to a borrower in accordance with this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(3)(d): (3)(b); (3)(c); (d) if known by the higher education institution, a corporation, partnership, joint venture, proprietorship, trust, association, or other entity that is created or organized pursuant to the laws of the United States or a state within the United States, if a majority of the stock or other equity interest is directly or indirectly owned by, or which derives a majority of its funding from:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(3)(e)(i): a foreign government;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(3)(e)(ii): (3)(b) an individual described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(3)(e)(iii): (3)(c); (d) an entity described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(4): "Gift" means an endowment, scholarship, gift, donation, or grant of money or property of any kind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(5): 53B-1-102 "Higher education institution" means an institution in the state system of higher education as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-201(6): (6)(a); (6)(a); (6)(a); (6)(c) "Restricted foreign entity" means:

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1): (1)(c); (2); (1)(a); (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(a): (1)(c); (2) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(b): A higher education institution may rely on the following address of a foreign person to determine the citizenship or nationality of the foreign person if the citizenship or nationality is unknown:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(b)(i): for a foreign person that is an individual, the principal residence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(b)(ii): for a foreign person that is not an individual, the principal place of business.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(c): (1)(a); (1)(a) The $50,000 amount described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(c)(i): with a principal residence or principal place of business located in the United States; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(c)(ii): with a permanent resident status:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(c)(ii)(A): under Section 245 of the Immigration and Nationality Act; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(1)(c)(ii)(B): for 10 years or more.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(d): (1) the aggregate amount of all gifts described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(f): for a conditional gift:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(f)(i): for a foreign person that is an individual, if known, the country of citizenship or principal residence of the individual; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(f)(ii): for a foreign person that is not an individual, if known, the country of incorporation or place of business of the foreign person; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(g): for a conditional gift that is a contract entered into between a higher education institution and a foreign person:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(g)(i): the amount;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(g)(ii): the date;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(g)(iii): a description of all conditions or restrictions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(2)(g)(iv): the name of the foreign person.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(3): A disclosure report required by this section is a public record open to inspection and review during the higher education institution's business hours.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(4): At the request of the board, the attorney general may file a civil action to compel a higher education institution to comply with the requirements of this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-202(6): Beginning July 1, 2023, a higher education institution may not seek or accept funding support from a restricted foreign entity or an entity that passes on funding support from a restricted foreign entity.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-401 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-401(1): 53B-1-402 "Board" means the Utah Board of Higher Education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-401(2): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" or "institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-401(3): "Miscarriage" means the spontaneous or accidental loss of a fetus, regardless of gestational age or the duration of the pregnancy.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402 Establishment of board -- Powers, duties, and authority -- Reports.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1): (1)(b)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a): There is established the Utah Board of Higher Education, which:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a)(i): is the governing board for the institutions of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a)(ii): controls, oversees, and regulates the Utah system of higher education in a manner consistent with the purpose of this title and the specific powers and responsibilities granted to the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b): (1)(b)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b)(i): The University of Utah shall provide administrative support for the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b)(ii): (1)(b)(i) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2): 53B-16-101; 53B-16-102; 53B-2-102; Chapter 7, Part 7, Performance Funding; Chapter 22, Part 2, Capital Developments; 53B-2a-117; 53B-2a-118; 53B-16-110; 53B-16-105; (2)(a); (c) The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a): establish and promote a state-level vision and goals for higher education that emphasize data-driven retrospective and prospective system priorities, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(i): quality;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(ii): affordability;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(iii): access and equity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(iv): completion;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(v): workforce alignment and preparation for high-quality jobs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(vi): economic growth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(b): establish system policies and practices that advance the vision and goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(c): establish metrics to demonstrate and monitor:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(c)(i): performance related to the goals; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(c)(ii): performance on measures of operational efficiency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(d): collect and analyze data including economic data, demographic data, and data related to the metrics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(e): govern data quality and collection across institutions;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(f): 53B-16-101 establish, approve, and oversee each institution's mission and role in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(g): assess an institution's performance in accomplishing the institution's mission and role;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(h): 53B-16-102 participate in the establishment and review of programs of instruction in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i): 53B-2-102 perform the following duties related to an institution of higher education president, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i)(i): 53B-2-102 appointing an institution of higher education president in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i)(ii)(A): providing support and guidance to an institution of higher education president; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i)(ii)(B): evaluating an institution of higher education president based on institution performance and progress toward systemwide priorities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i)(iii): setting the terms of employment for an institution of higher education president, including performance-based compensation, through an employment contract or another method of establishing employment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(i)(iv): establishing, through a public process, a statewide succession plan to develop potential institution presidents from within the system;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(j): Chapter 7, Part 7, Performance Funding; Chapter 22, Part 2, Capital Developments; 53B-2a-117; 53B-2a-118 create and implement a strategic finance plan for higher education, including by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(j)(i): establishing comprehensive budget and finance priorities for academic education and technical education;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(j)(iv): administering state financial aid programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(j)(v): Chapter 7, Part 7, Performance Funding administering performance funding in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(j)(vi): Chapter 22, Part 2, Capital Developments; 53B-2a-117; 53B-2a-118 developing a strategic capital facility plan and prioritization process in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(k): 53B-16-110; 53B-16-105; (2)(a); (c) create and annually report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on a seamless articulated education system for Utah students that responds to changing demographics and workforce, including by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(k)(i): 53B-16-110 providing for statewide prior learning assessment, in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(k)(vii): coordinating work-based learning; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(k)(viii): (2)(a); (c) emphasizing the system priorities and metrics described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(l): coordinate with the public education system:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(l)(i): regarding public education programs that provide postsecondary credit or certificates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(l)(ii): to ensure that an institution of higher education providing technical education serves secondary students in the public education system;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(m): delegate to an institution board of trustees certain duties related to institution governance including:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(m)(ii): effective administration;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(m)(iii): the institution's responsibility for contributing to progress toward achieving systemwide goals; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(m)(iv): other responsibilities determined by the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(n): delegate to an institution of higher education president management of the institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(o): consult with an institution of higher education board of trustees or institution of higher education president before acting on matters pertaining to the institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(p): maximize efficiency throughout the Utah system of higher education by identifying and establishing shared administrative services, beginning with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(p)(i): commercialization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(p)(ii): services for compliance with Title IX of the Education Amendments of 1972, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1681 et seq.;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(p)(iii): information technology services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(p)(iv): human resources, payroll, and benefits administration;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(q): develop strategies for providing higher education, including career and technical education, in rural areas;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(r): manage and facilitate a process for initiating, prioritizing, and implementing education reform initiatives, beginning with common applications and direct admissions;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(s): provide ongoing quality review of programs ; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(t): before each annual legislative general session, provide to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee a prioritization of all projects and proposals for which the board or an institution of higher education seeks an appropriation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(3): The board shall submit an annual report of the board's activities and performance against the board's goals and metrics to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(3)(a): the Education Interim Committee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(3)(b): the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(3)(c): the governor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(3)(d): each institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4): The board shall prepare and submit an annual report detailing the board's progress and recommendations on workforce related issues, including career and technical education, to the governor and to the Legislature's Education Interim Committee by October 31 of each year, including information detailing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(a): how institutions of higher education are meeting the career and technical education needs of secondary students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(b): how the system emphasized high demand, high wage, and high skill jobs in business and industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(c): performance outcomes, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(c)(i): entered employment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(c)(ii): job retention; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(c)(iii): earnings;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(d): an analysis of workforce needs and efforts to meet workforce needs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(4)(e): student tuition and fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(5): The board may modify the name of an institution of higher education to reflect the role and general course of study of the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(6): The board may not take action relating to merging a technical college with another institution of higher education without legislative approval.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(7): This section does not affect the power and authority vested in the State Board of Education to apply for, accept, and manage federal appropriations for the establishment and maintenance of career and technical education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9): 78B-6-103; Title 78B, Chapter 15, Part 8, Gestational Agreement The board shall adopt a policy requiring institutions to provide at least three work days of paid bereavement leave for an employee:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9)(a): following the end of the employee's pregnancy by way of miscarriage or stillbirth; or

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9)(b)(i): the employee is the individual's spouse or partner;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9)(b)(ii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9)(b)(ii)(A): the employee is the individual's former spouse or partner; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(9)(b)(ii)(B): the employee would have been a biological parent of a child born as a result of the pregnancy;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-403 Committees.
-------------------------------------------
The board may form committees to support the board in fulfilling the board's duties.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405 Qualifications for board members.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1): The board shall develop qualifications for the composition of the board to ensure that combined, the board members have:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(a): a range of experience, including experience in industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(b): varied areas of expertise; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(c): varied geographic representation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2): In developing the qualifications, the board shall consider:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a): expertise in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(i): business or industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(ii): technical education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(iii): general education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(iv): advanced education and research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(b): geographic representation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c): knowledge or experience in a field including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(i): finance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(ii): accounting or auditing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(iii): law;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(iv): facilities or real estate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(v): educational delivery models;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(vi): workforce development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(vii): economic development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(viii): kindergarten through grade 12 education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(ix): educational quality assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(3): The board shall consult with the governor to develop the qualifications described in this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-409 Appointment and hiring of staff.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-409(1): The commissioner may appoint and hire a staff of professional, legal, and administrative personnel.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-409(2): The commissioner shall determine salaries, retirement provisions, and other benefits for the staff described in this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410 Utah Board of Higher Education successor to rights and duties.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(1): The board is the successor to the Utah System of Technical Colleges Board of Trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2): For the Utah System of Technical Colleges Board of Trustees, the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(a): is vested with all rights, titles, privileges, powers, obligations, liabilities, immunities, franchises, endowments, assets, property, and claims;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(b): shall fulfill and perform all obligations, including obligations relating to outstanding bonds and notes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(c): may continue an administrative rule.

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101 Institutions of higher education -- Corporate bodies -- Powers.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1): The following institutions of higher education are bodies politic and corporate with perpetual succession and with all rights, immunities, and franchises necessary to function as such:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1)(a): the University of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1)(b): Utah State University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1)(c): Weber State University;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(2)(b): An institution of higher education is vested with all the property, franchises, and endowments of, and is subject to, all the contracts, obligations, and liabilities of the institution's respective predecessor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103 Degree-granting institution board of trustees -- Powers and duties.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(1): A degree-granting institution has a board of trustees that may act on behalf of the institution in performing duties, responsibilities, and functions as may be specifically authorized to the board of trustees by the board or by statute.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2): 53B-16-102 A board of trustees of a degree-granting institution has the following powers and duties:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(a): to facilitate communication between the institution and the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(b): to assist in planning, implementing, and executing fund raising and development projects aimed at supplementing institutional appropriations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(c): to perpetuate and strengthen alumni and community identification with the degree-granting institution's tradition and goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(d): to select recipients of honorary degrees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(e): 53B-16-102 to approve changes to the degree-granting institution's programs, in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3): 53B-1-402 A board of trustees of a degree-granting institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a): 53B-1-402 approve a strategic plan for the institution of higher education that is aligned with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(i): state attainment goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(ii): workforce needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(iii): 53B-1-402 board goals and metrics described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(iv): the institution of higher education's role, mission, and distinctiveness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(b): monitor the institution of higher education's progress toward achieving the strategic plan.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106 Duties and responsibilities of the president of a degree-granting institution of higher education -- Approval by board of trustees.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1): As used in this section, "president" means the president of a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(a): The president of each degree-granting institution may exercise grants of power and authority as delegated by the board, as well as the necessary and proper exercise of powers and authority not specifically denied to the degree-granting institution or the degree-granting institution's administration, faculty, or students by the board or by law, to ensure the effective and efficient administration and operation of the degree-granting institution consistent with the statewide strategic plan for higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b): A president may, after consultation with the degree-granting institution's board of trustees, exercise powers relating to the degree-granting institution's employees, including faculty and persons under contract with the degree-granting institution, by implementing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(i): furloughs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(ii): reductions in force;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(iii): benefit adjustments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(iv): program reductions or discontinuance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(v): early retirement incentives that provide cost savings to the degree-granting institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2)(b)(vi): other measures that provide cost savings to the degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3): (3)(a)(i) A president may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a): (3)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(i): appoint a secretary, a treasurer, administrative officers, deans, faculty members, and other professional personnel;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(ii): (3)(a)(i) prescribe duties for a position described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(iii): appoint support personnel;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(iv): prescribe duties for support personnel;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(v): determine salaries for support personnel from the degree-granting institution's position classification plan, which may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(v)(A): be based upon similarity of duties and responsibilities within the institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(v)(B): as funds permit, provide salary and benefits comparable with private enterprise;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vi): adopt policies for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vi)(A): employee sick leave use and accrual; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vi)(B): service recognition for employees with more than 15 years of employment with the degree-granting institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vii): subject to the authority of, the policy established by, and the approval of the board, and recognizing the status of the institutions within the Utah system of higher education as bodies politic and corporate, appoint attorneys to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vii)(A): provide legal advice to the degree-granting institution's administration; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a)(vii)(B): coordinate legal affairs within the degree-granting institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(b): subject to the approval of the degree-granting institution's board of trustees, provide for the constitution, government, and organization of the faculty and administration, and enact implementing rules, including the establishment of a prescribed system of tenure;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(c): subject to the approval of the degree-granting institution's board of trustees, authorize the faculty to determine the general initiation and direction of instruction and of the examination, admission, and classification of students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d): enact rules for administration and operation of the degree-granting institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(i): are consistent with the degree-granting institution's role established by the board, rules enacted by the board, or the laws of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(ii): may provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(ii)(A): administrative, faculty, student, and joint committees with jurisdiction over specified institutional matters;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(ii)(B): student government and student affairs organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(ii)(C): the establishment of institutional standards in furtherance of the ideals of higher education fostered and subscribed to by the degree-granting institution and the degree-granting institution's administration, faculty, and students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(d)(ii)(D): the holding of classes on legal holidays, other than Sunday.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4): A president shall manage the president's degree-granting institution as a part of the Utah system of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5): (3)(a)(vii); (3)(a)(vii); (3)(a)(vii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(a): (3)(a)(vii) Compensation costs and related office expenses for an attorney described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(b): (3)(a)(vii) The board shall coordinate the activities of attorneys described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c): (3)(a)(vii) An attorney described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c)(i): may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c)(i)(A): conduct litigation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c)(i)(B): settle a claim covered by the State Risk Management Fund; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c)(i)(C): issue a formal legal opinion; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c)(ii): shall cooperate with the Office of the Attorney General in providing legal representation to a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(d): A degree-granting institution shall submit an annual report to the board on the activities of appointed attorneys.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6): The board shall establish guidelines relating to the roles and relationships between presidents and boards of trustees, including those matters which must be approved by a board of trustees before implementation by the president.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7): A president is subject to regular review and evaluation administered by the board, in consultation with the degree-granting institution's board of trustees, through a process approved by the board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110 Utah Valley University -- Institutional name change.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(1): Beginning July 1, 2008, Utah Valley State College shall be known as Utah Valley University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2): The university is a continuation of Utah Valley State College and shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2)(a): possess all rights, title, privileges, powers, immunities, franchises, endowments, property, and claims of the college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2)(b): fulfill and perform all obligations of the college, including obligations relating to outstanding bonds and notes.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 2a - Technical Education
******************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-100.5 Title.
-----------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Technical Education."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(1): 63A-5b-401 "Capital development" means the same as capital development project, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(2): "Competency-based" means mastery of subject matter or skill level, as demonstrated through business and industry approved standards and assessments, achieved through participation in a hands-on learning environment, and which is tied to observable, measurable performance objectives.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(3): 53B-2a-118 "Dedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from the Technical Colleges Capital Projects Fund created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(4): 53B-2a-118 "Nondedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from a source other than the Technical Colleges Capital Projects Fund created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(5): 63A-5b-401 "State funds" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106 Technical colleges -- Duties.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1): (1)(a) Each technical college shall, within the geographic area served by the technical college:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(a): offer technical education programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b): (1)(a) offer a program described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b)(i): low cost to adult students, as approved by the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b)(ii): no tuition to secondary students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(c): develop cooperative agreements with school districts, charter schools, other higher education institutions, businesses, industries, and community and private agencies to maximize the availability of instructional facilities within the geographic area served by the technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d): after consulting with school districts and charter schools within the geographic area served by the technical college:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(i): ensure that secondary students in the public education system have access to technical education at the technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii): prepare and submit an annual report to the board detailing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(A): how the technical education needs of secondary students within the region are being met;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(B): what access secondary students within the region have to programs offered at the technical college;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(C): how the technical college emphasizes high demand, high wage, high skill jobs in business and industry; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(D): student tuition and fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2): 53E-3-501; 53F-4-504 A technical college may offer:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(a): 53E-3-501 a competency-based high school diploma approved by the State Board of Education in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(b): basic instruction in areas such as reading, language arts, and mathematics that are necessary for student success in a chosen technical education or job-related program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(c): courses of interest when similar offerings to the community are limited and courses are financially self-supporting; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(d): 53F-4-504 secondary school level courses through the Statewide Online Education Program in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3): (2)(d); (2)(b); (c); (5) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(a): (2)(b); (c) offer courses other than technical education or the basic instruction described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(b): offer a degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(c): (5) offer technical education or basic instruction outside the geographic area served by the technical college without a cooperative agreement between an affected institution of higher education, except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(d): provide tenure or academic rank for its instructors; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(e): participate in intercollegiate athletics.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(4): The mission of a technical college is limited to technical education and may not expand to include academic programs that lead to a degree.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5): (3)(c); (5)(a)(ii); (5)(a)(iii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a): (3)(c); (5)(a)(ii) A technical college may offer technical education or basic instruction outside the geographic area served by the technical college without a cooperative agreement, as required in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i): the technical education or basic instruction is specifically requested by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i)(A): an employer; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i)(B): a craft, trade, or apprenticeship program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(ii): the technical college notifies the affected institution about the request; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(iii): (5)(a)(ii) the affected institution is given an opportunity to make a proposal, prior to any contract being finalized or training being initiated by the technical college, to the employer, craft, trade, or apprenticeship program about offering the requested technical education or basic instruction, provided that the proposal shall be presented no later than one business week from the delivery of the notice described under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(b): (5)(a)(iii) The requirements under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107 Technical college presidents.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(1): 53B-2-102 The board shall appoint a president for each technical college in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2)(a): A technical college president is the chief executive officer of the technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2)(b): A technical college president:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2)(b)(i): does not need to have a doctorate degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2)(b)(ii): shall have extensive experience in career and technical education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3): A technical college president shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(a): exercise grants of power and authority as delegated by the board, as well as the necessary and proper exercise of powers and authority not specifically denied to the technical college's administration, faculty, or students, by the board or by law, to ensure the effective and efficient administration and operation of the technical college consistent with the statewide strategic plan for higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(b): administer the day-to-day operations of the technical college;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(c): consult with the technical college board of trustees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(d): administer human resource policies and employee compensation plans in accordance with the requirements of the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(e): prepare a budget request for the technical college's annual operations to the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(f): after consulting with the board, other institutions of higher education, school districts, and charter schools within the technical college's region, prepare a comprehensive strategic plan for delivering technical education within the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(g): consult with business, industry, the Department of Workforce Services, the Governor's Office of Economic Opportunity, and the Governor's Office of Planning and Budget on an ongoing basis to determine what workers and skills are needed for employment in Utah businesses and industries;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(h): coordinate with local school boards, school districts, and charter schools to meet the technical education needs of secondary students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(i): develop policies and procedures for the admission, classification, instruction, and examination of students in accordance with the policies and accreditation guidelines of the board and the State Board of Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(j): manage the technical college president's institution as part of the Utah system of higher education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6):

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b)(iv): An executive committee shall report the executive committee's activities to the technical college board of trustees at the technical college board of trustees' next regular meeting following the activities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(7): A technical college board of trustees may establish advisory committees.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110 Technical college board of trustees' powers and duties.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1): 53B-16-102; 53B-1-402 A technical college board of trustees shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(a): assist the technical college president in preparing a budget request for the technical college's annual operations to the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(b): after consulting with the board, other higher education institutions, school districts, and charter schools within the technical college's region, assist the technical college president in preparing a comprehensive strategic plan for delivering technical education within the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(c): 53B-16-102 in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(d): adopt an annual budget and fund balances;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(e): conduct annual program evaluations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f): 53B-1-402
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i): 53B-1-402 approve a strategic plan for the technical college that is aligned with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(A): state attainment goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(B): workforce needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(C): the technical college's role, mission, and distinctiveness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(D): 53B-1-402 board goals and metrics described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(ii): monitor the technical college's progress toward achieving the strategic plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(g): act on behalf of the technical college in performing other duties as authorized by the board or by statute.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(2): A technical college board of trustees may not exercise jurisdiction over career and technical education provided by a school district or charter school or provided by a higher education institution independently of the technical college.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112 Technical colleges -- Relationships with other public and higher education institutions -- Agreements -- Priorities -- New capital facilities.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1): As used in this section, "higher education institution" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a): Utah State University for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a)(i): Bridgerland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a)(ii): Tooele Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a)(iii): Uintah Basin Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(b): Weber State University for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(b)(i): Ogden-Weber Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(b)(ii): Davis Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(c): Utah Valley University for Mountainland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(d): Southern Utah University for Southwest Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(e): Utah Tech University for Dixie Technical College.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2): A technical college may enter into agreements:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2)(a): with other higher education institutions to cultivate cooperative relationships; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2)(b): with other public and higher education institutions to enhance career and technical education within the technical college's region.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3): Before a technical college develops new instructional facilities, the technical college shall give priority to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(a): maintaining the technical college's existing instructional facilities for both secondary and adult students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b): coordinating with the president of the technical college's degree-granting partner and entering into any necessary agreements to provide career and technical education to secondary and adult students that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b)(i): maintain and support existing higher education career and technical education programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b)(ii): maximize the use of existing higher education facilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(c): developing cooperative agreements with school districts, charter schools, other higher education institutions, businesses, industries, and community and private agencies to maximize the availability of career and technical education instructional facilities for both secondary and adult students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4): (3)(a); (c)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a): (3)(a); (c) Before submitting a funding request pertaining to new capital facilities and land purchases to the board, a technical college shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a)(i): (3)(a); (c) ensure that all available instructional facilities are maximized in accordance with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a)(ii): coordinate the request with the president of the technical college's degree-granting partner, if applicable.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(b): The Division of Facilities Construction and Management shall make a finding that the requirements of this section are met before the Division of Facilities Construction and Management may consider a funding request from the board pertaining to new capital facilities and land purchases for a technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(c): A technical college may not construct, approve the construction of, plan for the design or construction of, or consent to the construction of a career and technical education facility without approval of the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5): Before acquiring new fiscal and administrative support structures, a technical college shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(a): review the use of existing public or higher education administrative and accounting systems, financial record systems, and student and financial aid systems for the delivery of education in the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(b): determine the feasibility of using existing systems; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(c): with the approval of the technical college board of trustees and the board, use the existing systems.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113 Technical colleges -- Leasing authority -- Lease-purchase agreements -- Report.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1): A technical college may enter into a lease with other higher education institutions, school districts, charter schools, state agencies, or business and industry for a term of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(a): one year or less with the approval of the technical college board of trustees; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b): more than one year with the approval of the board if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b)(i): the Legislature approves funding for the lease prior to a technical college entering into the lease; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b)(ii): the lease agreement includes language that allows termination of the lease without penalty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a): A technical college may enter into a lease-purchase agreement if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(i): there is a long-term benefit to the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(ii): the project is included in the technical college master plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(iii): the lease-purchase agreement includes language that allows termination of the lease;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(iv): the lease-purchase agreement is approved by the technical college board of trustees and the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v): the lease-purchase agreement is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v)(A): reviewed by the Division of Facilities Construction and Management; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v)(B): approved by the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b): (2)(a) An approval under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(i): all parties, dates, and elements of the agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(ii): the equity or collateral component that creates the benefit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(iii): the options dealing with the sale and division of equity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3)(a): Each technical college shall provide an annual lease report to the board that details each of the technical college's leases, annual costs, location, square footage, and recommendations for lease continuation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3)(b): The board shall compile and distribute an annual combined lease report for all technical colleges to the Division of Facilities Construction and Management and to others upon request.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 3 - Enforcement of Regulations at Institutions
****************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101 Purpose of chapter.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101(1): It is the purpose of this chapter to confirm and clarify the power vested in the board to pass rules and regulations governing parking and traffic on campuses and related facilities and to enforce the rules and regulations by all appropriate methods.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101(2): The board may delegate this authority and other authority granted under this chapter to the president of each institution so long as the rules and regulations are approved by the institution's board of trustees.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102 State institution of higher education defined.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(1): 53B-2-101 As used in this chapter, "state institution of higher education" means an institution described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2): A state institution of higher education includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2)(a): a branch or affiliated institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2)(b): a campus or facilities owned, operated, or controlled by the governing board of the state institution of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103 Power of board to adopt rules and enact regulations.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(1): The board may enact regulations governing the conduct of university and college students, faculty, and employees.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-104 Establishment of police or security departments.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board may establish and maintain police or security departments for the purpose of enforcing the regulations of each institution of higher education and the laws of the state.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105 Appointment of police or security personnel -- Powers.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(1): Members of the police or security department of any college or university are appointed by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(2): Upon appointment, they are peace officers and have all the powers possessed by policemen in cities and by sheriffs, including the power to make arrests on view or on warrant of violation of state statutes and city or county ordinances.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(3): Members of the police or security department of any college or university also have the power to enforce all rules and regulations promulgated by the board as related to the institution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106 Criminal and traffic laws in full force and effect.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(1): All of the criminal laws of this state, including the traffic laws, are in full force and effect on the campuses of state institutions of higher education and upon all other property or facilities owned by the institutions or operated or controlled by the governing board of the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2): Title 41, Chapter 6a, Traffic Code
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2)(a): State institutions of higher education are "political subdivisions" and the board of the institutions is a "local authority."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2)(b): Title 41, Chapter 6a, Traffic Code All streets, roadways, alleys, and parking lots on property owned or controlled by state institutions of higher education are "streets or highways" as these terms are used in


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107 Traffic violations -- Notice of rule or regulation.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(1): It is a violation of this section for any person to operate or park a vehicle upon any property owned or controlled by a state institution of higher education contrary to posted signs authorized by the published rules and regulations of the institution or to block or impede traffic through or on any of these properties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(2): (1) A violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(3): Notice of a rule or regulation to all persons is sufficient if the rule or regulation is published in one issue of a newspaper of general circulation in the county or counties in which the institution and the campus or facility is located.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-108 Violation of chapter a misdemeanor.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
A violation of this chapter is a class B misdemeanor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-109 Jurisdiction of district and justice courts.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Any district court or any justice court of any city or county in which property owned or controlled by a state institution of higher education is located has jurisdiction to hear and determine cases involving an alleged violation of this chapter.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-110 Fines and forfeitures -- Disposition.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
All fines and forfeitures collected by any justice court judge and one-half of all the fines and forfeitures collected by the clerk of any district court for a violation of any of this chapter are remitted to the state treasurer to be credited to the general operating fund of the state institution of higher education complaining of the violation.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 4 - Compact for Western Regional Cooperation - Interstate Commission for Higher Education
***********************************************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-101 WICHE compact.
----------------------------------------------
As empowered by law, the governor of Utah has duly entered into a compact the text of which is as follows:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103 Commissioners -- Duties -- Records of academic progress -- Cancellation of student registration.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(1): The commissioners are the three resident members from the state of Utah, required by Article IV of the compact, and are authorized to function as representatives of the state on the Western Interstate Commission for Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2): The commissioners' duties are as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(a): to study the need for professional and graduate educational facilities not available within this state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(b): to recommend appropriations to meet the needs of this act;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(c): to provide for screening of all applicants for professional, graduate, or higher educational study not available within the state in accordance with established rules; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(d): to certify to out of state institutions under the compact all acceptable candidates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(3): An applicant may not be certified unless the applicant has been a bona fide resident of the state for at least the five years prior to the date of application.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4)(a): Students must maintain continuous Utah residency during their attendance at an out of state institution in order to receive financial support under the compact.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4)(b): If Utah residency is terminated by a student during any academic year in which the student has received financial support under the compact, the support shall be relinquished and terminated at the end of that academic year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5)(a): The Commissioner of Higher Education shall maintain records of the academic progress of Utah students receiving financial support under the compact while attending out of state institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5)(b): If the records reveal a student is not progressing satisfactorily, upon recommendation of the out of state institution, the commissioner shall cancel the student's registration and withhold future payments otherwise due.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 6 - Master Planning
*************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-102 Standardized systems prescribed by the board.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board shall prescribe for all institutions under its jurisdiction standardized systems of accounts, records, and reports covering in sufficient detail the operations of the educational institutions under its control.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104 Multi-University Consortium for Teacher Training in Sensory Impairments -- Purposes -- Appropriation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1)(a): In conjunction with the board's master plan for higher education, there is established a Multi-University Consortium for Teacher Training in Sensory Impairments which is an outgrowth of a consortium established by the federal government.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1)(b): The consortium shall include within its membership the University of Utah, Utah State University, Brigham Young University, the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind, the Services for At-Risk Students section under the State Board of Education, and local school districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(2): The consortium, in collaboration with the board and the State Board of Education, shall develop and implement teacher preparation programs that qualify and certify instructors to work with students who are visually impaired, deaf, or hard of hearing, or both visually impaired and deaf or hard of hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(3): The board shall consider including within the board's annual budget recommendations a line item appropriation to provide ongoing funding for the programs provided pursuant to this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-105.5 Technology Initiative Advisory Board -- Composition -- Duties.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-105.5(1): 53B-6-105 There is created a Technology Initiative Advisory Board to assist and make recommendations to the board in the board's administration of the Engineering and Computer Science Initiative established under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(a): (3) Subject to Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(b)(v): enrollment growth.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(c): The board's recommendations shall be available for presentation to the governor and to the Legislature at least 30 days before the convening of the Legislature, and shall include schedules showing the recommended amounts for each institution, including separately funded programs or divisions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(d): The recommended appropriations shall be determined by the board only after the board has reviewed the proposed institutional operating budgets, and has consulted with the various institutions and board staff in order to make appropriate adjustments.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(a): The budget recommendations of the board shall be accompanied by full explanations and supporting data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b): The appropriations recommended by the board shall be made with the dual objective of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b)(i): justifying for higher education institutions appropriations consistent with their needs, and consistent with the financial ability of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b)(ii): determining an equitable distribution of funds among the respective institutions in accordance with the aims and objectives of the statewide master plan for higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(a): The board shall request a hearing with the governor on the recommended appropriations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(b): After the governor delivers his budget message to the Legislature, the board shall request hearings on the recommended appropriations with the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(c): If either the total amount of the state appropriations or its allocation among the institutions as proposed by the Legislature or the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee is substantially different from the recommendations of the board, the board may request further hearings with the Legislature or the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee to reconsider both the total amount and the allocation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(7): The board may devise, establish, periodically review, and revise formulas for the board's use and for the use of the governor and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee in making appropriation recommendations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(8)(a): The board shall recommend to each session of the Legislature the minimum tuitions, resident and nonresident, for each institution which it considers necessary to implement the budget recommendations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(8)(b): The board may fix the tuition, fees, and charges for each institution at levels the board finds necessary to meet budget requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(9): Money allocated to each institution by legislative appropriation may be budgeted in accordance with institutional work programs approved by the board, provided that the expenditures funded by appropriations for each institution are kept within the appropriations for the applicable period.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(10): The dedicated credits, including revenues derived from tuitions, fees, federal grants, and proceeds from sales received by the institutions are appropriated to the respective institutions to be used in accordance with institutional work programs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(11): An institution may do the institution's own purchasing, issue the institution's own payrolls, and handle the institution's own financial affairs under the general supervision of the board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-102 Fiscal year.
--------------------------------------------
The fiscal year for each institution and for the board begins on July 1 and ends on June 30 in each year.
