Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5 Uses of revenue for athletic gender equity.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Beginning on July 1, 1998, a state institution of higher education shall annually use for the purposes described in Title IX of the Education Amendments of 1972, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1681 et seq., an amount of revenue equal to the total amount of sales and use tax revenue collected underUtah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5(1): during the one-year period beginning on July 1, 1997, and ending on June 30, 1998; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5(2): on amounts paid for admission to athletic events at the institution of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104 Retention of net reimbursed overhead revenues.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104(1): For fiscal year 1990-91 and for each succeeding year, all budget documents for the system of higher education shall reflect retention by the institutions within the system of their net reimbursed overhead revenues for support of research and related programs under policies established by the board. These overhead revenues may not be considered a dedicated credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104(2): The board, in conjunction with institutions within the system, shall provide the Legislature, through the Office of Legislative Fiscal Analyst, with a complete accounting of the net reimbursed overhead revenues on an annual basis.  This accounting shall include actual expenditures for the prior fiscal year, budgeted expenditures for the current fiscal year, and planned expenditures for the following fiscal year.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106 Personal use expenditures for officers and employees of institutions of higher education.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1): 53B-1-102; 51-7-3 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(a): "Employee" means a person who is not an elected or appointed officer and who is employed on a full- or part-time basis by an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution that is part of the state system of higher education as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(c): "Officer" means a person who is elected or appointed to an office or position within an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i): "Personal use expenditure" means an expenditure made without the authority of law that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(A): is not directly related to the performance of an activity as an officer or employee of an institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(B): primarily furthers a personal interest of an officer or employee of an institution of higher education or the family, a friend, or an associate of an officer or employee of an institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(C): would constitute taxable income under federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii): "Personal use expenditure" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii)(A): a de minimis or incidental expenditure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii)(B): a state vehicle or a monthly stipend for a vehicle that an officer or employee uses to travel to and from the officer or employee's official duties, including a minimal allowance for a detour as provided by the institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(e): 51-7-3 "Public funds" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2): An officer or employee of an institution of higher education may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2)(a): use public funds for a personal use expenditure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2)(b): incur indebtedness or liability on behalf of, or payable by, an institution of higher education for a personal use expenditure.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3): (2); (3)(b) If the institution of higher education determines that an officer or employee of an institution of higher education has intentionally made a personal use expenditure in violation of Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(a)(i): the personal use expenditure was disbursed; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(a)(ii): payment for the indebtedness or liability for a personal use expenditure was disbursed;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(b): require the officer or employee to remit an administrative penalty in an amount equal to 50% of the personal use expenditure to the institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(c): (3)(b) deposit the money received under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501 Purpose.
----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(1): The Legislature recognizes that community colleges and established branch campuses and centers throughout the state have a special mission to provide comprehensive higher education opportunities for financially needy students, at geographically disbursed locations and at favorable tuition rates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(2): The Legislature further recognizes that tuition and general fee costs to students at Utah community colleges and established branch campuses and centers represent significant challenges for many of the students they serve, and that additional scholarship money for financially needy students attending those institutions is needed to ensure financial access to higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(3): It is the purpose of this part to establish a program of matching grants as an incentive for institutions to raise money for scholarships at community colleges, branch campuses, and centers.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704 Designation of targeted jobs -- Determination of estimated revenue growth from targeted jobs -- Reporting.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1): As used in this section, "baseline amount" means the average annual wages for targeted jobs over calendar years 2014, 2015, and 2016, as determined by the Department of Workforce Services using the best available information.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2): (2)(d)(ii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a): The Department of Workforce Services shall designate, as a targeted job, a job that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(i): has a base employment level of at least 100 individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(ii): ranks in the top 20% of jobs for outlook based on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(ii)(A): projected number of openings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(ii)(B): projected rate of growth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(iii): ranks in the top 20% of jobs for median annual wage; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a)(iv): requires postsecondary training.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(b): The Department of Workforce Services shall designate targeted jobs every other year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(c): The GO Utah office may, after consulting with the Department of Workforce Services and industry representatives, designate a job that has significant industry importance as a targeted job.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(d): (2)(d)(ii) Annually, the Department of Workforce Services and the GO Utah office shall report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on targeted jobs, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(d)(i): the method used to determine which jobs are targeted jobs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(d)(ii): changes to which jobs are targeted jobs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(d)(iii): (2)(d)(ii) the reasons for each change described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3): (2); (3)(a); (3)(b) Based on the targeted jobs described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3)(a): determining the total estimated wages for targeted jobs for the year:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3)(a)(i): based on the average wages for targeted jobs, calculated using the most recently available wage data and data from each of the two years before the most recently available data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3)(a)(ii): using the best available information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3)(b): (3)(a) determining the change in estimated wages for targeted jobs by subtracting the baseline amount from the total wages for targeted jobs described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(3)(c): (3)(b) multiplying the change in estimated wages for targeted jobs described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(4): Annually, at least 30 days before the first day of the legislative general session, the Department of Workforce Services shall report the estimated revenue growth from targeted jobs to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(4)(a): the Office of the Legislative Fiscal Analyst; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(4)(b): the Division of Finance.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709 Five-year performance goals.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(A); 53B-7-706(2)(c); 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(C); 53B-1-102; 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(B) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(a): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(A) "Access metric" means the metric described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(b): "Award" means a degree or certificate that an institution grants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(c): "Cohort" means a group of students, defined by the year in which the group enrolls in an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(d): "Five-year performance period" means the five-year period beginning on July 1, 2022, and ending on June 30, 2027.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(e): 53B-7-706(2)(c) "High-yield award" means the same as that term is defined in board policy under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(f): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(C) "High-yield awards metric" means the metric described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(g): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(h): "Standard completion time" means the time in which a student typically completes an award program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(i): "System" means the Utah System of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(j): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(B) "Timely completion metric" means the metric described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2): 53B-7-706(1)(a)(ii) The goals established by the board in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(a): for the access metric, to increase the percent of Utah high school graduates participating in the system by 3.0%;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(b): for the timely completion metric, to increase the system percentage of a cohort that completes an award in up to and including 1.5 times the standard completion time by 3.0%; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(c): for the high-yield awards metric, to increase the system percentage of high-yield awards by 3.0%.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3): (2) In order to meet the system goals described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(a): for the access metric, to increase the institution's share of Utah high school graduates participating in the system by a percentage that the board determines;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(b): for the timely completion metric, to increase the percent of a cohort enrolled at the institution that completes an award in up to and including 1.5 times the standard completion time or sooner by a percentage that the board determines; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(c): for the high-yield awards metric, to increase the percent of high-yield awards the institution grants by a percentage that the board determines.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-801 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "endowment"  means the Higher Education Student Success Endowment created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802 Higher Education Student Success Endowment.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(1): There is created the Higher Education Student Success Endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2): The endowment consists of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(a): the proceeds from divestment of the dissolved Utah Higher Education Assistance Authority's loan portfolio;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(b): appropriations made to the endowment by the Legislature, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(c): income from the investment of the endowment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(d): other revenues received from other sources.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(3): The board shall account for the receipt and expenditures of endowment money in accordance with the policies and guidance of the Division of Finance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a)(i): The state treasurer shall invest the endowment money with the primary goal of providing for stability, income, and growth of the principal.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a)(ii): The state treasurer may deduct any administrative costs incurred in managing endowment assets from earnings before distributing the earnings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(b): Nothing in this section requires a specific outcome in investing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(c): The state treasurer may employ professional asset managers to assist in the investment of assets of the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(d): The state treasurer may only provide compensation to asset managers from earnings generated by the endowment's investments.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e): The state treasurer shall invest and manage the endowment assets as a prudent investor would, by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e)(i): considering the purposes, terms, distribution requirements, and other circumstances of the endowment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e)(ii): exercising reasonable care, skill, and caution in order to meet the standard of care of a prudent investor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f): In determining whether or not the state treasurer has met the standard of care of a prudent investor, the judge or finder of fact shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f)(i): consider the state treasurer's actions in light of the facts and circumstances existing at the time of the investment decision or action, and not by hindsight; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f)(ii): evaluate the state treasurer's investment and management decisions respecting individual assets not in isolation, but in context of an endowment portfolio as a whole as a part of an overall investment strategy that has risk and return objectives reasonably suited to the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5)(a): The endowment shall earn interest.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5)(b): The state treasurer shall deposit the interest or other revenue earned from investment of the endowment into the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6): 53B-1-402(2)(a); 53B-2-101 The board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a): 53B-1-402(2)(a); 53B-2-101 may expend money from the endowment for programs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a)(i): 53B-1-402(2)(a) advance the system priorities as established in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a)(ii): 53B-2-101 support prospective students or current students enrolled at an institution, as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(b): may not expend money from the endowment for a capital expenditure, including the construction or lease of a capital facility or operation and maintenance of a capital facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7): 53B-1-402(2)(a) The board shall ensure that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7)(a): 53B-1-402(2)(a) money deposited into the endowment is irrevocable and is expended only for programs that advance the system priorities as established in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7)(b): creditors of the board of directors may not seize, attach, or otherwise obtain assets of the endowment.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803 Board duties.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1): 53B-7-802 The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(a): act as trustee of the endowment and exercise the state's fiduciary responsibilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(b): meet at least twice a year to conduct business on behalf of the endowment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(c): review and approve all endowment policies, projections, rules, criteria, procedures, forms, standards, and performance goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(d): 53B-7-802 review and approve the budget and expenditures for the endowment in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(e): review financial records for the endowment, including endowment receipts, expenditures, and investments; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(f): take any other action necessary to perform the board's fiduciary obligations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(2): The board shall annually submit a budget and expenditures to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee no later than November 1.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-804 State grants to the authority.
--------------------------------------------------------------
To the extent otherwise allowed, a state entity may grant money or property to the endowment.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-805 Gifts to the endowment.
-------------------------------------------------------
A person may make a contribution, gift, grant, bequest, or devise, or loans to the endowment.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-102(3): (3)(a)(iii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-102(3)(a): Institutions within the state system of higher education may grant resident student status to any student who has come to Utah and established residency for the purpose of attending an institution of higher education, and who, prior to registration as a resident student:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-102(3)(b)(vii): a rental agreement showing the student's name and Utah address for at least 12 months prior to application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-102(3)(b)(viii): utility bills showing the student's name and Utah address for at least 12 months prior to application.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103 Waiver of nonresident differential in tuition rates -- Utah Tech University good neighbor tuition waivers.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1): (1)(a)(i); (1)(a) Notwithstanding any other provision of law:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a): (1)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(i): The board may determine when to grant a full or partial waiver of the nonresident differential in tuition rates charged to undergraduate students pursuant to reciprocal agreements with other states.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(ii): (1)(a)(i) In making the determination described under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(ii)(A): enhance educational opportunities for Utah residents;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(ii)(B): promote mutually beneficial cooperation and development of Utah communities and nearby communities in neighboring states;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(ii)(C): contribute to the quality of educational programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(a)(ii)(D): assist in maintaining the cost effectiveness of auxiliary operations in Utah institutions of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(b): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(b)(i): (1)(a) Consistent with its determinations made pursuant to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(b)(ii): An agreement shall provide for the numbers and identifying criteria of undergraduate students, and shall specify the institutions of higher education that will be affected by the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(c): The board shall establish policy guidelines for the administration by the affected Utah institutions of any tuition waivers authorized under this section, for evaluating applicants for such waivers, and for reporting the results of the reciprocal waiver programs authorized by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(1)(d): A report and financial analysis of any waivers of tuition authorized under this section shall be submitted annually to the general session of the Legislature as part of the budget recommendations of the board for the system of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(a): Utah Tech University may offer a good neighbor full waiver of the nonresident differential in tuition rates charged to undergraduate students:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(a)(i): pursuant to reciprocal agreements with other states; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(a)(ii): to a resident of a county that has a portion of the county located within 70 miles of the main campus of Utah Tech University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(b)(i): A student who attends Utah Tech University under a good neighbor tuition waiver shall pay a surcharge per credit hour in addition to the regular resident tuition and fees of Utah Tech University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(b)(ii): The surcharge per credit hour shall be based on a percentage of the approved resident tuition per credit hour each academic year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(b)(iii): The percentage assessed as a surcharge per credit hour shall be set by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(c): Utah Tech University may restrict the number of good neighbor tuition waivers awarded.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103(2)(d): A student who attends Utah Tech University on a good neighbor tuition waiver may not count the time during which the waiver is received towards establishing resident student status in Utah.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5 Alumni legacy nonresident scholarships.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(1): In addition to other nonresident tuition scholarships, the president of an institution may waive an amount up to the full nonresident portion of tuition for alumni legacy nonresident scholarships.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(2): The purposes of alumni legacy nonresident scholarships are to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(2)(a): assist in maintaining an adequate level of service and related cost-effectiveness of auxiliary operations in institutions of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(2)(b): promote enrollment of nonresident students with high academic aptitudes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(2)(c): recognize the legacy of past graduates and promote a continued connection to their alma mater.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(3): To qualify for an alumni legacy scholarship, a student shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(3)(a): enroll at an institution within the state system of higher education for the first time; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-103.5(3)(b): have at least one parent or grandparent who graduated with an associate's degree or higher from the same institution in which the student is enrolling.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104 Nonresident partial tuition scholarships.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(1): The board may grant a scholarship for partial waiver of the nonresident portion of total tuition charged by public institutions of higher education to nonresident undergraduate students, subject to the limitations provided in this section, if the board determines that the scholarship will:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(1)(a): promote mutually beneficial cooperation between Utah communities and nearby communities in states adjacent to Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(1)(b): contribute to the quality and desirable cultural diversity of educational programs in Utah institutions;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(1)(c): assist in maintaining an adequate level of service and related cost-effectiveness of auxiliary operations in Utah institutions of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(1)(d): promote enrollment of nonresident students with high academic aptitudes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(2): The board shall establish policy guidelines for the administration by institutions of higher education of any partial tuition scholarships authorized under this section, for evaluating applicants for those scholarships, and for reporting the results of the scholarship program authorized by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(3): (2) The policy guidelines promulgated by the board under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(3)(a): the amount of the approved scholarship may not be more than 1/2 of the differential tuition charged to nonresident students for an equal number of credit hours of instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(3)(b): a nonresident partial tuition scholarship may be awarded initially only to a nonresident undergraduate student who has not previously been enrolled in a college or university in Utah and who has enrolled full time for 10 or more credit hours, whose legal domicile is within approximately 100 highway miles of the Utah system of higher education institution at which the recipient wishes to enroll or such distance that the board may establish for any institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(3)(c): the total number of nonresident partial tuition scholarships granted may not exceed a total of 600 such scholarships in effect at any one time; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(3)(d): the board shall determine eligibility for nonresident partial tuition scholarships on the basis of program availability at an institution and on a competitive basis, using quantifiable measurements such as grade point averages and results of test scores.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104(4): The board shall submit an annual report and financial analysis of the effects of offering nonresident partial tuition scholarships authorized under this section to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee as part of the board's budget recommendations for the system of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5 Nonresident tuition scholarships.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(1): 53B-8-104; 53B-8-102 In addition to the scholarships authorized under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(1)(a): assist in maintaining an adequate level of service and related cost-effectiveness of auxiliary operations in Utah institutions of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(1)(b): promote enrollment of nonresident students with high academic aptitudes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(1)(c): 53B-8-102 provide for an effective transition to meet the requirements of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(2): (1); (1) The board shall establish policy guidelines for the administration by institutions of higher education of scholarships authorized under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3): (2); (1) The policy guidelines promulgated by the board under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(a): a maximum of 675 of the approved scholarships may be up to 100% of the differential tuition charged to nonresident students for an equal number of credit hours of instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(b): 225 of the approved scholarships may not be at a level of more than 50% of the differential tuition charged to nonresident students for an equal number of credit hours of instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(c): a nonresident scholarship may be awarded initially only to a nonresident student who has not previously been enrolled in a college or university in Utah and who has enrolled full time for 10 or more credit hours;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(d): (1) the total number of nonresident scholarships granted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(e): the board shall determine eligibility for nonresident scholarships on the basis of program availability at an institution and appropriate academic credentials, using quantifiable measurements such as grade point averages and results of test scores; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(3)(f): a nonresident student who receives a scholarship of greater than 50% of the differential tuition charged to nonresident students for an equal number of credit hours of instruction may not be counted against the funded target for the institution attended.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(4): The board shall submit an annual report and financial analysis of the effects of offering nonresident tuition scholarships authorized under this section to the Legislature as part of its budget recommendations for the system of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-104.5(5): This section applies to tuition scholarships and not the individual admission standards of higher education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106 Resident tuition -- Requirements -- Rules.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(1): If allowed under federal law, a student, other than a nonimmigrant alien within the meaning of paragraph (15) of subsection (a) of Section 1101 of Title 8 of the United States Code, shall be exempt from paying the nonresident portion of total tuition if the student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(1)(a): attended high school in this state for three or more years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(1)(b): graduated from a high school in this state or received the equivalent of a high school diploma in this state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(1)(c): registers as an entering student at an institution of higher education not earlier than the fall of the 2002-03 academic year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(2): (1) In addition to the requirements under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(3): The board shall make rules for the implementation of this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-106(4): Nothing in this section limits the ability of institutions of higher education to assess nonresident tuition on students who do not meet the requirements under this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107 Military member surviving dependents -- Tuition waiver.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1): Title 39A, National Guard and Militia Act As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(a): "Federal active duty" means serving under orders in accordance with United States Code, Title 10 or Title 32, at any time on or after September 11, 2001.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b): "Qualifying deceased military member" means a person who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b)(i): was killed while serving on state or federal active duty, under orders of competent authority and not as a result of the member's own misconduct; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b)(ii): dies of wounds or injuries received while serving on state or federal active duty, under orders of competent authority and not as a result of the member's own misconduct; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b)(iii): was a member of the armed forces of the United States and a Utah resident;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b)(iv): was a member of the reserve component of the armed forces on or after September 11, 2001, and a Utah resident; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(b)(v): was a member of the Utah National Guard on or after September 11, 2001.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(1)(c): Title 39A, National Guard and Militia Act "State active duty" means serving in the Utah National Guard in any duty status authorized by the governor under
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(2): This section shall be known as the Scott B. Lundell Military Survivors' tuition waiver.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3): (4); 53B-8-102 A state institution of higher education shall waive undergraduate tuition for a dependent of a qualifying deceased military member under the following conditions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3)(a): the dependent has been accepted by the institution in accordance with the institution's admissions guidelines;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3)(b): (4); 53B-8-102 except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3)(c): the dependent may not have already completed a course of studies leading to an undergraduate degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3)(d): the dependent may only utilize the waiver for courses that are applicable toward the degree or certificate requirements of the program in which the dependent is enrolled; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(3)(e): the dependent may not be excluded from the waiver if the dependent has previously taken courses at or has been awarded credit by a state institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(4): (3)(b); 53B-8-102 Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(5): The tuition waiver in this section is applicable for undergraduate study only.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(6): The Department of Veterans and Military Affairs, after consultation with the adjutant general if necessary, shall certify to the institution that the dependent is a surviving dependent eligible for the tuition waiver in accordance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(7): The waiver in this section does not apply to fees, books, or housing expenses.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-107(8): The board may request reimbursement from the Legislature for costs incurred in providing the tuition waiver under this section.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 8a - Utah Educational Savings Plan
****************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101 Purpose.
-----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(1)(a): The Legislature finds that the general welfare and well-being of the state are directly related to educational levels and skills of the citizens of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(1)(b): Therefore, a vital and valid public purpose is served by the creation and implementation of programs which encourage and make possible the attainment of higher education by the greatest number of citizens of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(2)(a): The Legislature finds that the state has limited resources to provide additional programs for higher education funding and that the continued operation and maintenance of the state's public institutions of higher education and the general welfare of the citizens of the state will be enhanced by establishing a plan which allows citizens of the state to invest money in a public trust for future application to the payment of higher education costs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(2)(b): (2)(a) The Legislature further finds that the plan described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(3)(a): In order to make available to the citizens of the state an opportunity to fund future higher education needs, it is necessary that a public trust be established in which money may be invested for future educational use.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-101(3)(b): It may also be necessary to establish and create an endowment fund, which may be funded with public funds, among other sources, the income from which may be made available to account owners to enhance or encourage their savings invested for future higher education costs or for use in scholarship or other college savings incentive programs.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102 Definitions for chapter.
---------------------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102(1): "Account agreement" means an agreement between an account owner and the Utah Educational Savings Plan entered into under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102(2): "Account owner" means a person, estate, or trust, if that person, estate, or trust has entered into an account agreement under this chapter to save for the higher education costs on behalf of a beneficiary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102(3): "Beneficiary" means the individual designated in an account agreement to benefit from the amount saved for higher education costs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102(4): 53B-8a-103 "Plan" means the Utah Educational Savings Plan created in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5 Definitions for part.
--------------------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(1): "Administrative fund" means the money used to administer the Utah Educational Savings Plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(2): 53B-8a-105 "Board" means the Utah Education Savings Board of Trustees created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(3): 53B-8a-107 "Endowment fund" means the endowment fund established under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(4): "Executive director" means the administrator appointed to administer and manage the Utah Educational Savings Plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(5): "Federally insured depository institution" means an institution whose deposits and accounts are to any extent insured by a federal deposit insurance agency, including the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation and the National Credit Union Administration.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(6): "Grantor trust" means a trust, the income of which is for the benefit of the grantor under Section 677, Internal Revenue Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(7): "Higher education costs" means qualified higher education expenses as defined in Section 529(e)(3), Internal Revenue Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(8): "Owner of the grantor trust" means one or more individuals who are treated as an owner of a trust under Section 677, Internal Revenue Code, if that trust is a grantor trust.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(9): 53B-8a-107 "Program fund" means the program fund created under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(10): "Qualified investment" means an amount invested in accordance with an account agreement established under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-102.5(11): "Tuition and fees" means the quarterly or semester charges imposed to attend an institution of higher education and required as a condition of enrollment.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103 Creation of Utah Educational Savings Plan -- Powers and duties of plan -- Certain exemptions.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(1): There is created the Utah Educational Savings Plan, which may also be known and do business as:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(1)(a): the Utah Educational Savings Plan Trust; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(1)(b): another related name.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2): The plan:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2)(a): is a non-profit, self-supporting agency that administers a public trust;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2)(b): shall administer the various programs, funds, trusts, plans, functions, duties, and obligations assigned to the plan:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2)(b)(i): consistent with sound fiduciary principles; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2)(b)(ii): subject to review of the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(2)(c): shall be known as and managed as a qualified tuition program in compliance with Section 529, Internal Revenue Code, that is sponsored by the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3): 53B-8a-107 The plan may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(a): make and enter into contracts necessary for the administration of the plan payable from plan money, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(a)(i): contracts for goods and services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(a)(ii): contracts to engage personnel, with demonstrated ability or expertise, including consultants, actuaries, managers, counsel, and auditors for the purpose of rendering professional, managerial, and technical assistance and advice;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(b): adopt a corporate seal and change and amend the corporate seal;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(c): 53B-8a-107 invest money within the program, administrative, and endowment funds in accordance with the provisions under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(d): enter into agreements with account owners, any institution of higher education, any federal or state agency, or other entity as required to implement this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(e): solicit and accept any grants, gifts, legislative appropriations, and other money from the state, any unit of federal, state, or local government, or any other person, firm, partnership, or corporation for deposit to the administrative fund, endowment fund, or the program fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(f): make provision for the payment of costs of administration and operation of the plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(g): carry out studies and projections to advise account owners regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(g)(i): present and estimated future higher education costs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(g)(ii): levels of financial participation in the plan required to enable account owners to achieve their educational funding objective;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(h): participate in federal, state, local governmental, or private programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(i): create public and private partnerships, including investment or management relationships with other 529 plans or entities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(j): promulgate, impose, and collect administrative fees and charges in connection with transactions of the plan, and provide for reasonable service charges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(k): procure insurance:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(k)(i): against any loss in connection with the property, assets, or activities of the plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(k)(ii): indemnifying any member of the board from personal loss or accountability arising from liability resulting from a member's action or inaction as a member of the plan's board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(l): administer outreach efforts to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(l)(i): market and publicize the plan and the plan's products to existing and prospective account owners; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(l)(ii): encourage economically challenged populations to save for post-secondary education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(m): adopt, trademark, and copyright names and materials for use in marketing and publicizing the plan and the plan's products;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(n): administer the funds of the plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(o): sue and be sued in the plan's own name;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(p): own institutional accounts in the plan to establish and administer:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(p)(i): scholarship programs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(p)(ii): other college savings incentive programs, including programs designed to enhance the savings of low income account owners investing in the plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(3)(q): have and exercise any other powers or duties that are necessary or appropriate to carry out and effectuate the purposes of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(4): (4)(b); Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act; 53B-8a-111; 67-3-12
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(4)(a): (4)(b); Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(4)(b): 53B-8a-111; 67-3-12

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-103(4)(b)(ii): 67-3-12 Financial information that is provided by the plan to the state auditor and posted on the public finance website established by the state auditor in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-104 Office facilities, clerical, and administrative support for the Utah Educational Savings Plan.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-104(1): The Utah Board of Higher Education shall provide to the plan, by agreement, administrative support and office facilities and space.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-104(2): Reasonable charges or fees may be levied against the plan pursuant to the agreement for the services provided by the Utah Board of Higher Education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105 Powers and duties of board.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(1): There is created the Utah Education Savings Board of Trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2): (2)(a) The Utah Board of Higher Education shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a): appoint the members of the board as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(i): not more than three members from the Utah Board of Higher Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii): at least four public members, each of whom possesses skills in one or more of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(A): investments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(B): accounting;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(C): finance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(D): banking;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(E): education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(F): technology; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(a)(ii)(G): financial operations; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(2)(b): (2)(a) designate a member appointed under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(3): Each board member serves at the pleasure of the Utah Board of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(4): The board has all powers necessary to carry out and effectuate the purposes, objectives, and provisions of this chapter pertaining to the plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(5): The board shall act as a fiduciary of the plan with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(5)(a): a duty of care to act solely in the best interest of the plan's account owners and beneficiaries;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(5)(b): a duty of loyalty putting the plan's interest ahead of other interests; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(5)(c): a duty to invest with care, skill, prudence, and diligence.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(6): The duties, responsibilities, funds, liabilities, and expenses of the board in oversight and governance of the plan shall be maintained separate and apart from the Utah Board of Higher Education's other duties, responsibilities, funds, liabilities, and expenses.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(7): The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(7)(a): make policies governing the administration of the plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(7)(b): amend policies related to board governance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(8)(a): The board may appoint advisory committees to aid the board in fulfilling its duties and responsibilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(8)(b): An advisory committee member may receive compensation and be reimbursed for reasonable expenses incurred in the performance of the member's official duties as determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(9): (6) The board may appoint a board of directors known as the Board of Directors of the Utah Education Savings Plan to carry out the obligation of separation of functions required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(10): (9) If the board creates a board of directors under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(10)(a): the board of directors shall consist of at least five members; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-105(10)(b): no more than two-thirds of the members of the board of directors may simultaneously serve as a member of the board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(4)(c): an account owner may not borrow from the plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(5): The execution of an account agreement by the plan may not guarantee in any way that higher education costs will be equal to projections and estimates provided by the plan or that the beneficiary named in any account agreement will:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(5)(d): graduate from the institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(6): A beneficiary may be changed as permitted by the rules and regulations of the board upon written request of the account owner prior to the date of admission of any beneficiary under an account agreement by an institution of higher education so long as the substitute beneficiary is eligible for participation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(7): An account agreement may be freely amended throughout the term of the account agreement in order to enable an account owner to increase or decrease the level of participation, change the designation of beneficiaries, and carry out similar matters as authorized by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(8): Each account agreement shall provide that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(8)(a): the account agreement may be canceled upon the terms and conditions, and upon payment of the fees and costs set forth and contained in the board's rules and regulations; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-106(8)(b): the executive director may amend the agreement unilaterally and retroactively, if necessary, to maintain the plan as a qualified tuition program under Section 529, Internal Revenue Code.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107 Program, administrative, and endowment funds -- Investment and payments from funds -- Proxy voting -- State treasurer access.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(1): The plan shall segregate money received by the plan into three funds, the program fund, the administrative fund, and the endowment fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2): Title 75, Chapter 7, Part 9, Utah Uniform Prudent Investor Act The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(a): Title 75, Chapter 7, Part 9, Utah Uniform Prudent Investor Act invest the plan in a manner that is consistent with the prudent investor rule for trustees established in
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(b): in accordance with the board's fiduciary responsibilities, make investment decisions with the sole purpose of maximizing the risk-adjusted return on the investments; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(c): to the extent practicable:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(c)(i): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(c)(i)(A): retain the right to vote investor proxies; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(c)(i)(B): if the investments are commingled with another investor's funds, request the right to vote investor proxies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(2)(c)(ii): ensure proxy voting is exercised to maximize risk-adjusted returns for the exclusive benefit of beneficiaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(3): 53B-8a-103; 53B-8a-105 Transfers may be made from the program fund to the administrative fund to pay operating costs:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(3)(a): 53B-8a-103; 53B-8a-105 associated with administering the plan and as required under Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(3)(b): as included in the budget approved by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(a): All money paid by account owners in connection with account agreements shall be deposited as received into separate accounts within the program fund which shall be invested and accounted for separately.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(b): Money accrued by account owners in the program fund may be used for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(b)(i): payments to any institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(b)(ii): payments to the account owner or beneficiary;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(b)(iii): transfers to another 529 plan; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(4)(b)(iv): other expenditures or transfers made in accordance with the account agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(a): All money received by the plan from the proceeds of gifts and other endowments for the purposes of the plan shall be:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(a)(i): deposited, according to the nature of the donation, as received into the endowment fund or the administrative fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(a)(ii): invested and accounted for separately.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(b): Any gifts, grants, or donations made by any governmental unit or any person, firm, partnership, or corporation to the plan for deposit to the endowment fund or the administrative fund is a grant, gift, or donation to the state for the accomplishment of a valid public eleemosynary, charitable, and educational purpose and is not included in the income of the donor for Utah tax purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(c): The endowment fund or the administrative fund may be used to enhance the savings of low income account owners investing in the plan, for scholarships, or for other college savings incentive programs as approved by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(d): Transfers may be made between the endowment fund and the administrative fund upon approval by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(5)(e): Endowment fund earnings not accruing to a beneficiary under an account agreement, not transferred to the administrative fund, or not otherwise approved by the board for expenditure, shall be reinvested in the endowment fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(6): (2) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(7)(a): The board shall make proxy voting records available to the state treasurer upon the state treasurer's request.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-107(7)(b): The state treasurer is subject to the same restrictions on disclosure of the proxy voting records as the board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108 Cancellation of agreements.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(1): Any account owner may cancel an account agreement at will.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(2): (3) If an account agreement is cancelled by the account owner, the current account balance shall be disbursed to the account owner less:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(2)(a): (3) an administrative refund fee, which may be charged by the plan, except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(2)(b): any penalty or tax required to be withheld by the Internal Revenue Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(3): An administration refund fee may not be levied by the plan if the account agreement is cancelled due to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(3)(a): the death of the beneficiary; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-108(3)(b): the permanent disability or mental incapacity of the beneficiary.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109 Repayment and ownership of funds in the account -- Transfer of ownership rights.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(a): The account owner retains ownership of funds in the account until:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(a)(i): funds are used to pay higher education costs for the beneficiary;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(a)(ii): funds are otherwise disbursed;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(a)(iii): funds are transferred for administrative costs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(a)(iv): the account is closed.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(1)(b): Funds in the account shall be considered to be held in trust for the benefit of the beneficiary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(2): Any amounts that may be paid pursuant to the plan that are not listed in this section are owned by the plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(3)(a): An account owner may transfer ownership rights to another eligible person.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-109(3)(b): The transfer shall be affected and the property distributed in accordance with administrative regulations promulgated by the board or the terms of the account agreement.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-110 Effect of payments on determination of need and eligibility for student aid.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
No student loan program, student grant program, or other program administered by any agency of the state, except as may be otherwise provided by federal law or the provisions of any specific grant applicable to that law, shall take into account and consider amounts available for the payment of higher education costs pursuant to the plan in determining need and eligibility for student aid.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111 Annual audit of financial statements -- Information to governor and Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111(1): The financial statements of the plan shall be audited annually by the state auditor or the state auditor's designee and reported in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111(2): The plan shall submit to the governor and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111(2)(a): upon request, any studies or evaluations of the plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111(2)(b): upon request, a summary of the benefits provided by the plan including the number of participants and beneficiaries in the plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-111(2)(c): upon request, any other information which is relevant in order to make a full, fair, and effective disclosure of the operations of the plan.

----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-112(1): 59-10-201 For tax purposes the property of the plan and its income are governed by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-112(2): (1) The tax commission, in consultation with the board and the plan, may adopt rules necessary to monitor and implement the tax provisions referred to in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-113 Property rights to plan assets.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-113(1): The assets of the plan, including the program fund and the endowment fund, shall at all times be preserved, invested, and expended solely and only for the purposes of the plan and shall be held in trust for the account owners and beneficiaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-113(2): No property rights in the plan shall exist in favor of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-113(3): The assets may not be transferred or used by the state for any purposes other than the purposes of the plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-114 Liberal construction.
------------------------------------------------------
This chapter shall be construed liberally in order to effectuate its legislative intent.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(1): "529 savings account" means a tax-advantaged method of saving for higher education costs on behalf of a particular individual that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(1)(a): meets the requirements of Section 529, Internal Revenue Code; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(1)(b): is managed by the plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(2): "Child" means an individual less than 20 years of age.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(3): "Community partner" means a nonprofit organization that provide services to a child who is economically disadvantaged or a family member, legal guardian, or legal custodian of a child who is economically disadvantaged.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(4): "Donation" means a gift, grant, donation, or any other conveyance of money by a person other than the Legislature that is not made directly for the benefit or on behalf of a particular individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(5): "Economically disadvantaged" means that a child is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(5)(a): experiencing intergenerational poverty;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(5)(b): a member or foster child of a family with an annual income at or below 185% of the federal poverty level;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(5)(c): living with a legal custodian or legal guardian with an annual family income at or below 185% of the federal poverty level; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(5)(d): living with a legal custodian or legal guardian who can attest that the child or the child's household is receiving services benefitting low-income households or individuals.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(6): "Eligible individual" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(6)(a): is under 20 years of age and is a resident of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(6)(b): is economically disadvantaged; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(6)(c): receives, or has a family member, a foster family member, or a legal custodian or legal guardian who receives, services from a community partner.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(7): "Federal poverty level" means the poverty level as defined by the most recently revised poverty income guidelines published by the United States Department of Health and Human Services in the Federal Register.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(8): 53B-8a-102.5 "Higher education costs" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(8)(a): a credit-granting institution of higher education within the state system of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(8)(b): a private, nonprofit college or university in the state that is accredited by the Northwestern Association of Schools and Colleges; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(8)(c): a technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(9): 35A-9-102 "Intergenerational poverty" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-201(10): 53B-8a-202 "Program" means the Student Prosperity Savings Program created in Section

----------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-203(2)(b)(ii): the amount of the donation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-203(2)(b)(iii): the date on which the person makes the donation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8a-203(2)(c): The date on which the person makes a donation to the program is the date on which the plan receives the donation, unless the plan receives the donation on a Saturday, a Sunday, or a holiday, in which case the date on which the person makes the donation shall be the first business day after the day on which the plan receives the donation.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 8c - Police Officer's and Firefighter's Survivor Tuition Act
******************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Police Officer's and Firefighter's Survivor Tuition Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(1): "Child" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(1)(a): is a natural or adopted child of a deceased peace officer or deceased firefighter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(1)(b): was under the age of 25 at the time of the peace officer's or firefighter's death.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(2): "Department" means the Department of Public Safety.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(3)(a): "Fees" means general course fees, in addition to tuition, that are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(3)(a)(i): imposed by a state institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(3)(a)(ii): required to be paid by a student to engage in a course of study at the state institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(3)(b): "Fees" does not include a special course fee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(4): "Killed" means that the peace officer's or firefighter's death is the direct and proximate result of a traumatic injury incurred in the line of duty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(5): "Line of duty" means an action that a peace officer or firefighter is obligated or authorized to perform by rule, regulation, condition of employment or service, or law, including a social, ceremonial, or athletic function that the peace officer or firefighter is assigned to or compensated for by the public agency being served.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(6): "Occupational disease" means a disease that routinely constitutes a special hazard in, or is commonly regarded as concomitant of, the peace officer's or firefighter's occupation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(7): 53B-1-102 "State institution of higher education" means those institutions designated in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(8): "Traumatic injury" means a wound or the condition of the body caused by external force, including an injury inflicted by bullet, explosive, sharp instrument, blunt object, or other physical blow, fire, smoke, chemical, electricity, climatic condition, infectious disease, radiation, or bacteria, but excluding an occupational disease.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(9): "Tuition" means tuition and fees at the rate charged for residents of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(10): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(10)(a): "Utah firefighter" or "firefighter" means a member, including volunteer members and members paid on call, of a fire department or other organization that provides fire suppression and other fire-related services, of a political subdivision who is responsible for or is in a capacity that includes responsibility for the extinguishment of fires.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(10)(b): "Utah firefighter" or "firefighter" does not include a person whose job description, duties, or responsibilities do not include direct involvement in fire suppression.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-102(11): "Utah peace officer" or "peace officer" means an employee of a law enforcement agency that is part of or administered by the state or any of its political subdivisions, and whose duties consist primarily of the prevention and detection of crime and the enforcement of criminal statutes or ordinances of this state or any of its political subdivisions.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103 Tuition waivers for surviving spouses and children of police officers and firefighters killed in the line of duty -- Qualifications -- Limitations.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1): (2); (3); (4); 53B-8-102; (2); (1)(c) Beginning in the 1997-98 academic year, and subject to the limitations in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(a): applies, qualifies, and is admitted as a full-time, part-time, or summer school student in a program of study leading to a degree or certificate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(b): 53B-8-102 is a resident student of the state as determined under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(c): (2) applies to the department for a waiver of tuition under this chapter and provides evidence satisfactory to the department that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(c)(i): the applicant is the surviving spouse or child of a peace officer or firefighter who was killed in the line of duty;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(c)(ii): (2) the course or courses for which the applicant is seeking a tuition waiver meet the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(c)(iii): the applicant meets the other requirements of this section;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(d): (1)(c) for a child of a peace officer or firefighter killed in the line of duty, applies under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(e): maintains satisfactory academic progress, as defined by the institution of higher education, for each term or semester in which the individual is enrolled, which may be measured by the definition used for federal student assistance programs under Title IV of the Higher Education Act of 1965; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(1)(f): has not achieved a bachelor's degree and has received tuition reimbursement under this chapter for less than 124 semester credits or 180 quarter credits at an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(2): A child or surviving spouse of a peace officer or firefighter who was killed in the line of duty is eligible for a tuition waiver under this section of not more than nine semesters or the equivalent number of quarters.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(3): Tuition shall be waived only to the extent that the tuition is not covered or paid by any scholarship, trust fund, statutory benefit, or any other source of tuition coverage available for a waiver under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-103(4): An institution of higher education shall waive tuition under this chapter only for courses that are applicable toward the degree or certificate requirements of the program in which the child or surviving spouse is enrolled.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-104 Notice of tuition waiver approval -- Annual appropriation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-104(1): 53B-8c-103(1)(c); 53B-8c-103 Upon receiving an application under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-104(2): The department shall provide the necessary forms and applications and cooperate with the state's institutions of higher education in developing efficient procedures for the implementation of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8c-104(3): The Legislature may annually appropriate the funds necessary to implement this chapter, including money to offset the tuition waivers at each institution.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8d-103 Tuition waivers for wards of the state.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8d-103(1): (2); (3); (4); 53B-8-102; (2); (1)(c) Beginning in the 2001-02 academic year, and subject to the limitations in Subsections

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8d-103(3)(a): after the individual has applied for financial assistance, including scholarships and Pell Grants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8d-103(3)(b): only to the extent that the tuition is not covered or paid by any scholarship, trust fund, statutory benefit, Pell Grant, or any other source of tuition coverage available for a waiver under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8d-103(4): An institution of higher education shall waive tuition under this chapter only for courses that are applicable toward the degree or certificate requirements of the program in which the student is enrolled.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 8e - Utah Purple Heart Recipients' Tuition Act
****************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8e-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Utah Purple Heart Recipients' Tuition Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8e-102 Definitions.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 9 - Higher Education for Senior Citizens
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-101 Legislative findings on higher education for senior citizens and veterans -- Legislative intent -- Quarterly registration fee.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-101(1): The Legislature finds that substantial benefits would accrue to the state, as well as those directly involved, through making higher education more accessible to senior citizens and veterans who generally find themselves with more time for learning but with less funds for such purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-101(2): 68-3-12.5 It is intended that an institution of higher education allow Utah residents who have reached 62 years of age or are veterans as defined in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-102 Enrollment on space-available basis -- Enrollment reports.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-102(1): Enrollment of senior citizens under this chapter is permissible after regularly enrolled students have been assigned and admitted to available classroom space in accordance with regular procedures and normal teaching loads in that space within the approved budget.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-102(2): Enrollments are determined by each institution under rules and guidelines promulgated by the board in accordance with findings of fact that space is available for the enrollments without increased instructional cost.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-102(3): Institutional enrollment reports shall show senior citizens separately, and they are not counted as full-time students.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-9-103 Rules.
--------------------------------------
The board may promulgate reasonable rules to carry out the purpose of this chapter.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203 Selection of qualifying jobs and qualifying degrees.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(1): Every other year, the GO Utah office shall select:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(1)(a): five qualifying jobs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(1)(a)(i): have the highest demand for new employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(1)(a)(ii): offer high wages; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(1)(b): the qualifying degrees for each qualifying job.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2): The GO Utah office shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2)(a): ensure that each qualifying job:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2)(a)(i): ranks in the top 40% of jobs based on an employment index that considers the job's growth rate and total openings;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2)(a)(ii): ranks in the top 40% of jobs for wages; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2)(a)(iii): requires an associate's degree or a bachelor's degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-10-203(2)(b): report the five qualifying jobs and qualifying degrees to the board.
