Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(A): electrical power generation, distribution, and utility-scale energy storage infrastructure and capacity, including reliability, cost, and availability standards;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(B): interconnected smart charging infrastructure, intelligent transportation systems, control systems, and communications systems to facilitate the transition to electrified transportation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(C): private surface transportation, including passenger vehicles, freight trucks, and freight trains;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(D): public surface transportation, including passenger vehicles, buses, and trains;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(E): air transportation, including private commercial aircraft and unmanned aircraft systems;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(F): vehicles that operate off-highway, including construction, mining, and agriculture;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(G): charging technology, solutions, and systems, including charging stations and shared use of infrastructure across modes of transportation and vehicle classes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(H): workforce, including analysis of the capacity and types of education, vocations, trades, and certifications necessary in each relevant sector to develop the local workforce needed to accomplish the vision; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iii)(I): any other sector that the steering committee determines is substantially necessary to fulfilling the stated mission;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(iv): (1)(b) identification of key gaps in the ecosystem from the sectors and industries described in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(v): evaluation of risk and vulnerability of relevant supply chains, including natural resources to ensure stability and availability; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(b)(vi): an accounting of funds appropriated to or received by the research center, and any expenditure of those funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(1)(c): (1) Before August 1, 2024, the research center shall report on the action plan described in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(2): (1)(b) Beginning in 2025, before August 1 of each year, the research center shall provide an annual report to the Infrastructure and General Government Appropriations Subcommittee of the Legislature, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(2)(a): (1)(b) an updated and prioritized list of strategic objectives identified in the initial report described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1806(2)(b): any actionable goals established or recommended by the research center;

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 19 - State Arboreta
*************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-19-101 Establishment of state arboreta -- Purpose.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In recognition of the cultural role that trees and shrubbery and birds and bees have played in the settlement and development of this state and the hardships that many of the pioneers endured to bring to this land seeds, plants, trees, and shrubs which have contributed so much to the scenic beauty of this state, it is deemed expedient that state arboreta be established for the purpose of further developing a knowledge and appreciation of trees and shrubs and to provide a place where they may be planted and cultivated as memorials and for the cultural enjoyment of the people of the state.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-19-102 Establishment of state arboreta at University of Utah and Utah State University.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
State arboreta are created and established at the University of Utah and Utah State University.  The universities may, on behalf of the people of this state, cultivate a greater knowledge and public appreciation for the trees and plants around us, as well as those growing in remote sections of the country and world.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-19-103 Acceptance of gifts by University of Utah and Utah State University.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The University of Utah and Utah State University are authorized to receive gifts, contributions, and donations of all kinds, including gifts and contributions of trees, plants, and shrubbery of every variety to promote the purposes and pursuits of an arboretum.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 20 - Property Rights - Title and Control
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-101 Property of institutions to vest in state board.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Utah Board of Higher Education is the successor to, and vested with, all the powers and authority relating to all properties, real and personal, tangible and intangible, and to the control and management of the property which was held by the governing board of each institution prior to the creation of the board.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-102 Vesting of rights, claims, and causes of action in higher education institutions -- Right to sue in corporate name.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
All rights, claims, and causes of action to or for any property vested in an institution of higher education prior to the effective date of this chapter, or the use of or income from the property, or for any conversion, disposition, and withholding of the property, or for any damage or injury to the property vests in the institution.  The institution may bring and maintain actions in its corporate name to recover, protect, and preserve all property and rights of the institution and enforce any contract relating to those rights and property.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103 Powers of state board -- Capital facilities projects -- Exceptions.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(1): As used in this section, "capital facilities projects and buildings" includes any one or more institutional projects and buildings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2): The board, on behalf of the institutions of higher education, may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(a): acquire, purchase, construct, improve, remodel, add to, and extend capital facilities projects and buildings including necessary and related utilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(b): accept buildings, land, or a combination of buildings and land, donated to an eligible higher education institution without obtaining approval of the donation from the director of the Division of Facilities Construction and Management;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(c): acquire necessary and suitable equipment, furnishings, and land for institutional projects and buildings;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(d): set aside portions of campuses for institutional projects and buildings;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(e): maintain and operate institutional projects and buildings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(2)(f): impose and collect rents, fees, and charges for the use of institutional projects and buildings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(3): Notwithstanding any other provision of law, if a donor donates land to an eligible institution of higher education and commits to build a building or buildings on that land, and the institution agrees to provide funds for the operations and maintenance costs from sources other than state funds, and agrees that the building or buildings will not be eligible for state capital improvement funding, the higher education institution may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(3)(a): oversee and manage the construction without involvement, oversight, or management from the Division of Facilities Construction and Management; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-103(3)(b): arrange for management of the project by the Division of Facilities Construction and Management.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104 Buildings and facilities -- Board approval of construction and purchases -- Rules.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(1): The board shall approve all new construction, repair, or purchase of educational and general buildings and facilities financed from any source at all institutions subject to the jurisdiction of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(2): An institution may not submit plans or specifications to the Division of Facilities Construction and Management for the construction or alteration of buildings, structures, or facilities or for the purchases of equipment or fixtures for the structure without the authorization of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(3): The board shall make rules establishing the conditions under which facilities may be eligible to request state funds for operations and maintenance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(4): (3) Before approving the purchase of a building, the board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(4)(a): (3) determine whether or not the building will be eligible for state funds for operations and maintenance by applying the rules adopted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-104(4)(b): if the annual request for state funding for operations and maintenance will be greater than $100,000, notify the speaker of the House, the president of the Senate, and the cochairs of the Infrastructure and General Government subcommittee of the Legislature's Joint Appropriation Committee.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-105 Institutional right to receive and convert grants, gifts, devises, or bequests.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-105(1): Each institution may convert property received by gift, grant, devise, or bequest, and not suitable for its use, into other property or into money. All property received or converted under this subsection shall be held, invested, and managed and the proceeds used for the purposes and under the conditions prescribed in the grant or donation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-105(2): If a condition is imposed by the terms of a grant, gift, devise, or bequest which is impracticable under the law, the grant is still valid. However, the condition must be rejected and the intent of the grantor carried out as nearly as may be possible.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-105(3): A grant, gift, devise, or bequest for the benefit of the institution is not defeated or prejudiced by any misnomer, misdescription, or informality, if the intent of the grantor or donor can be shown or ascertained with reasonable certainty.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-20-106 Property exempt from taxes and assessments.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
The property of the institutions governed by the board is exempt from all taxes and assessments.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 21 - Revenue Bonds
************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101 Financing of projects or buildings -- Issuance of bonds -- Sale price determined by board -- Payment of bonds -- Bonds exempt from income taxation.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(1): In order to pay all or part of the cost of the acquisition, purchase, construction, improvement, remodeling, addition to, extension, equipment, and furnishing of any project or building, including the acquisition of all necessary land, the board, on behalf of the institution for which this is to be done, may do the following: (a) borrow money on the credit of the income and revenues to be derived from the operation of the building, the imposition of student building fees, land grant interest, and net profits from proprietary activities, or from sources other than by appropriations by the Legislature to issuing institutions and, in anticipation of the collection of this income and revenues, issue negotiable bonds of the institution in an amount as the board determines is necessary for these purposes; and (b) provide for the payment of these bonds and the rights of their holders as provided in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(2): Bonds may: (a) be issued in one or more series; (b) bear any date or dates; (c) mature at any time or times not exceeding 40 years from their date; (d) be in any denominations; (e) be in any form, either coupon or registered; (f) carry registration and conversion privileges; (g) be executed in any manner; (h) be payable in any medium of payment at any place; (i) be subject to any terms of redemption with or without premium; and (j) bear interest at any rate or rates as provided by resolution adopted by the board at or before the sale of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(3): The bonds may be sold in a manner, at the lowest obtainable rate or rates of interest, and at a price or prices as determined by the board. These determinations are conclusive.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(4): The board may authorize one issue of bonds for the acquisition, purchase, construction, improvement, remodeling, adding to, extending, furnishing, or equipping of more than one building, including the acquisition of all necessary land, and may make the bonds payable from the combined revenues of all the buildings as well as from student building fees, land grant interest, net profits from proprietary activities, and from sources other than those derived from appropriations from the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(5): The bonds issued under this chapter have all of the qualities and incidents of negotiable paper and are not subject to state or local income taxation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-101(6): This section does not apply to a technical college.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102 Bonds do not create state indebtedness -- Special obligations -- Discharge of bonded indebtedness -- Agreements and covenants by the board regarding bonds -- Enforcement by court action.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1): 53B-21-101; 53B-21-111; (1)(c)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(a): The bonds issued under this chapter are not an indebtedness of the state, of the institution for which they are issued, or of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(b): 53B-21-101; 53B-21-111 They are special obligations payable solely from the revenues derived from the operation of the building and student building fees, land grant interest, net profits from proprietary activities, and any other revenues pledged other than appropriations by the Legislature as provided in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(c): (1)(c)(i)

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(c)(i)(B): meet projected shortfalls of payment of principal or interest or both for the following year on any bonds issued under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(c)(ii): (1)(c)(i) The governor may request from the Legislature an appropriation of the amount certified under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(d)(i): The state may not alter, impair, or limit the rights of bondholders or persons contracting with the board until the bonds, including interest and other contractual obligations, are fully met and discharged.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(1)(d)(ii): Nothing in this chapter precludes an alteration, impairment, or limitation if provision is made by law for the protection of bondholders or persons entering into contracts with the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(2): The board shall pledge all or any part of the revenues to the payment of principal of and interest on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3): In order to secure the prompt payment of principal and interest and the proper application of the revenues pledged, the board may, by appropriate provisions in the resolution authorizing the bonds:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(a): covenant as to the use and disposition of the proceeds of the sale of the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(b): covenant as to the operation of the building and the collection and disposition of the revenues derived from the operation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(c): collect student building fees from all students, and pledge the fees to the payment of building bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(d): covenant as to the rights, liabilities, powers, and duties arising from the breach of any covenant or agreement into which it may enter in authorizing and issuing the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(e): covenant and agree to carry insurance on the building, and its use and occupancy, and provide that the cost of any insurance is part of the expense of operating the building;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f): vest in a trustee:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f)(i): the right to receive all or any part of the income and revenues pledged and assigned to or for the benefit of the holder or holders of the bonds issued under this chapter, and to hold, apply, and dispose of the income and revenue; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f)(ii): the right to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f)(ii)(A): enforce any covenant made to secure the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f)(ii)(B): execute and deliver a trust agreement which sets forth the powers and duties and the remedies available to the trustee and limits the trustee's liabilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(f)(ii)(C): prescribe the terms and conditions upon which the trustee or the holders of the bonds in any specified amount or percentage may exercise such rights and enforce any or all covenants and resort to any appropriate remedies;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(g): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(g)(i): fix rents, charges, and fees, including student building fees, to be imposed in connection with and for the use of the building and its facilities, which are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(g)(i)(A): income and revenues derived from the operation of the building; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(g)(i)(B): expressly required to be fully sufficient either by themselves or with land grant interest and net profits from proprietary activities, or from sources other than by appropriations by the Legislature to such issuing institutions to assure the prompt payment of principal of and interest on the bonds as each becomes due; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(g)(ii): make and enforce rules with reference to the use of the building and with reference to requiring any class or classes of students to use the building as desirable for the welfare of the institution and its students or for the accomplishment of the purposes of this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(h): covenant to maintain a maximum percentage of occupancy of the building;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(i): covenant against the issuance of any other obligations payable from the revenues to be derived from the building, unless subordinated;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(j): make provision for refunding;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(k): covenant as to the use and disposition of sources of revenue other than those derived from appropriations by the Legislature, and pledge those sources of revenues to the payment of bonds issued under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(l): make other covenants considered necessary or advisable to effect the purposes of this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(m): delegate to the chair, vice-chair, or chair of the Budget and Finance Subcommittee the authority:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(m)(i): to approve any changes with respect to interest rate, price, amount, redemption features, and other terms of the bonds as are within reasonable parameters set forth in the resolution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(3)(m)(ii): to approve and execute all documents relating to the issuance of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(4)(a): The agreements and covenants entered into by the board under this section are binding in all respects upon the board and its officials, agents, and employees, and upon its successors.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-102(4)(b): They are enforceable by appropriate action or suit at law or in equity brought by any holder or holders of bonds issued under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-103 Agreements with federal government for funds.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board may enter into an agreement with the federal government in order to obtain funds for the following purposes: (1) to supplement bond proceeds used to pay for the projects referred to in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104 Deposit of bond proceeds -- Division of Facilities Construction and Management responsibilities and approval.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104(1): The board treasurer or other fiscal officer, with the approval of the state treasurer, deposits the proceeds from the sale of bonds under this chapter into a special Construction Trust Fund Account established in compliance with the State Money Management Act of 1974.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104(2): The proceeds are credited to the board on behalf of the institution of higher education for which the bonds were issued.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104(3): The proceeds are kept in a separate fund and used solely for the purpose for which they were authorized by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104(4): 53B-21-101 The Division of Facilities Construction and Management makes all contracts and executes all instruments which it considers necessary to provide for the projects referred to in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-104(5): The proceeds in the special Construction Trust Fund Account shall be disbursed only upon receipt of written statements supported by itemized estimates and claims presented to the Division of Facilities Construction and Management as provided in the resolution authorizing the issuance of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105 Disposition and use of income from operation of buildings -- Payment of principal and interest on bonds.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105(1): 53B-21-102(3)(f) Except for the revenues paid directly to a trustee under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105(2)(a): This money is for the payment of the principal and interest on the bonds authorized under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105(2)(b): The money shall also be used, to the extent provided in the resolution authorizing the bonds, to pay for the cost of maintaining and operating the building and to establish reserves for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-105(3): The board treasurer or other designated fiscal officer shall, not less than 15 days prior to the date interest and principal payments are due, transmit to the paying agent sufficient money from the fund to pay the obligation.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106 Examination and certification of bonds by attorney general -- Recital of certification -- Incontestability of bonds.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106(1): The resolutions and proceedings authorizing the issuance and confirming sale of bonds under this chapter are submitted to the attorney general for examination.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106(2): When the resolutions and proceedings have been examined and the bonds certified as legal obligations by the attorney general, the bonds are incontestable in any court in the state unless suit is brought within 30 days from the date of the approval.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106(3): A bond authorized under this section shall contain a recital on its face in substantially the following form: "This bond is one of a series of bonds which were certified as legal obligations by the attorney general of the state of Utah on ___."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106(4): Bonds authorized, issued, and sold under resolutions and proceedings approved by the attorney general are prima facie valid and binding obligations according to their terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-106(5): The only defense which may be offered in any suit instituted after the 30-day period has expired is forgery, fraud, or violation of the Constitution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-107 Investment in bonds by private and public entities -- Approval as collateral security.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-107(1): Any bank, savings and loan association, trust, or insurance company organized under the laws of this state or federal law may invest its capital and surplus in bonds issued under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-107(2): The officers having charge of a sinking fund or any county, city, metro township, town,, or school district may invest the sinking fund in bonds issued under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-107(3): The bonds shall also be approved as collateral security for the deposit of any public funds and for the investment of trust funds.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108 Financing project by contract or lease agreement instead of by bond issue -- Authority of board -- Term of lease -- Terms of agreement -- Board covenants.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(1): Whenever the board, by resolution, finds and declares it preferable to acquire a project under this chapter by purchase or lease of the facilities constituting the project under an agreement which provides the consideration for the purchase or lease to be paid in installments during a period not exceeding 99 years, rather than through the issuance of revenue bonds by the board in the manner provided in this chapter, it may do so upon compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(2): 53B-20-103 The board may lease, to any person, any portion of the campus of the institution necessary as a site for a project which the board is authorized to acquire under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(3): The agreement authorized to be entered into by the board shall provide that the person shall construct, improve, remodel, add to, or extend a project of the type and construction described in the agreement on the part of the campus to be leased to the person, or on such real property as may be acquired for that purpose by the person.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(4): The agreement shall further provide for the leasing of the project, including necessary equipment, furnishings, and land, from the person to the board executing the agreement, for a period not exceeding 99 years.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(5): Prior to the execution of the agreement, the person proposing to lease the project, including the necessary equipment, furnishings, and land, to the board shall submit to the board all plans, specifications, and estimates for the project.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(6): The plans, specifications, and estimates shall be approved by resolution of the board prior to the execution of the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7): The board may, by appropriate provisions in the agreement:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(a): covenant as to the use which will be made of the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(b): covenant as to the operation, maintenance, and supervision of the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(c): covenant to collect fees and charges from all students and other persons availing themselves of the use of the accommodations and facilities of the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(d): covenant to levy and collect student building fees from all regular and part-time students enrolled in the institution for the use and availability of the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(e): covenant as to the collection, use, and disposition of the proceeds arising from the collection of all the revenues, fees, and charges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(f): covenant to impose and collect fees and charges in amounts adequate to pay all costs incurred in maintaining and operating the project and to pay the amortization of the acquisition cost of the project, including necessary equipment and furnishings, and interest on the unpaid part of the acquisition cost, whether represented by rental installments or otherwise;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(g): covenant to pledge all revenues, fees, and charges, including student building fees, arising from the ownership and operation of the project to the payment of the rental installments provided for under the terms of the contract or lease agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(h): covenant as to the rights, liabilities, powers, and duties arising from the breach of any covenant or agreement contained in the agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(i): covenant and agree to carry any insurance on the project, and its use and occupancy, as the board considers desirable, and to provide that the cost of the insurance shall be included as a part of the cost of operating the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(j): covenant to make and enforce such parietal rules and regulations with reference to the use of the facilities comprising the project, or any part of the project, and with reference to requiring any class of students to use the project, or any part of the project, as the board determines desirable for the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(7)(k): covenant against the pledging of the revenues, fees, and charges, including student building fees, arising from the ownership and operation of the project for any purpose other than the payment of the rental installments required to be paid under the agreement, or against the issuance of any obligations payable therefrom, unless the pledge or obligations are made subordinate to the agreement.  Nothing in this section prevents the board from providing conditions and terms under which pledges may be made and obligations issued on a parity with the pledge of revenues, fees, and charges under the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(8): It shall be specifically provided in the agreement that the board is not obligated to pay the rental installments or amortization of the acquisition cost of the project, and interest on the unpaid part of the acquisition cost, from any source other than the revenues, fees, and charges arising from the ownership and operation of the project, including student building fees levied for the use and availability of the facilities of the project.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(9): Each agreement shall provide that the rental installments, or amortization of the acquisition cost of the project, including necessary equipment, furnishings, and land, and interest on the unpaid part of the acquisition cost, are not an obligation of the state, and that ad valorem taxes or appropriations from the state may not be used to pay or discharge the amounts required to be paid under the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(10): The agreement shall also provide that when the amortized acquisition cost, as represented by the rental installments, has been paid in full and when all obligations, if any, issued by the person to finance the cost of the acquisition of the project have been paid in full as to both principal and interest, the agreement terminates and title to the project, including the land upon which the project is situated, and all equipment and furnishings, vests in the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(11): The agreement may provide that the board may purchase the project, including the land upon which the project is situated, and all equipment and furnishings, which is subject to the agreement upon terms wherein rental installments previously made, or a portion of them, are deducted from the cost of acquisition of the project, including the land upon which the project is situated, and all equipment and furnishings, as provided for in the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(12): The board may furnish without charge heat, light, water, power, and similar facilities for any project leased by the board for operation by the board under this section, and all projects acquired and constructed under this section are exempt from taxation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(13): The agreement may provide that the board may lease the project, including the land upon which the project is situated, and all equipment and furnishings, to any person for a term not exceeding 99 years for operation by any person.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-108(14): A lease may not be entered into unless the rental to be paid to the board by the person is sufficient to satisfy the rental to be paid by the board to the person from which the project was originally leased.  But in no event may the rental paid to the board be less than the fair rental value of the property leased.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-109 Student building fees.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-109(1): The board issuing bonds under this chapter may impose and collect student building fees from all students in attendance at the institution in behalf of which the bonds are issued.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-109(2): The board may also pledge the fees in the same manner provided for the pledging of other revenues of the board or institution under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110 Refunding bonds -- Issuance -- Proceeds -- Limitations.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(1): Bonds may be issued under this chapter for the purpose of refunding any bonds previously issued under authority of this chapter, if the bonds to be refunded are due or callable, redeemable, or repurchasable by their terms on or prior to the date that the refunding bonds are issued or will become due or callable, redeemable, or repurchasable by their terms within 10 years thereafter or if the bonds to be refunded, even though not becoming due, callable, redeemable, or repurchasable within this period, are voluntarily surrendered by the bondholders for cancellation at the time of the issuance of the refunding bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(2): These refunding bonds shall have such details, bear such rate of interest, and be otherwise issued and secured as provided by the board authorizing the issuance of the bonds and as otherwise provided in this chapter.  However, the changes in the security and revenues pledged to the payment of the bonds may be made by the board as may be provided by it in the proceedings authorizing the bonds, but in no event shall the refunding bonds ever be secured by revenues not authorized by this chapter to be pledged to the payment of bonds issued for other than refunding purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(3): Refunding bonds issued under this chapter may be exchanged for a like principal amount of the bonds to be refunded, may be sold in the manner provided in this chapter for the sale of other bonds, or may be exchanged in part and sold in part.  If sold, the proceeds of the sale not required for the payment of expenses may be invested in United States Government obligations or in obligations unconditionally guaranteed by the United States of America in a manner as may be provided in the authorizing resolution, so long as these investments will mature with interest so as to provide funds to pay when due, or called for redemption, the bonds to be refunded together with interest and redemption premiums, if any.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(4): The proceeds or obligations shall, and other funds legally available to the board for such purposes may, be deposited in trust with an FDIC insured bank doing business in Utah, or its successor, to be held for the payment and redemption of bonds to be refunded.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(5): The deposit and any reinvestment shall be held in trust by the escrow agent for the payment of bonds with interest and redemption premiums, if any, on maturity or upon an available redemption date or upon an earlier voluntary surrender with the consent of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-110(6): No refunding bonds may be issued under this section in a principal amount in excess of the principal amount of the bonds to be refunded nor may any bonds not maturing or callable for redemption under their terms as provided in this section be refunded without the consent of the holders of the bonds.  Refunding bonds authorized and issued under this section may in the discretion of the board be combined with other bonds to be authorized and issued under this chapter, and a single issue of bonds may be authorized, part for improvement and part for refunding purposes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111 Authorized loans for acquisition, construction, furnishing, and equipping of projects -- Evidence of indebtedness -- Provisions -- Agreements with lending institutions -- Satisfaction and discharge -- Exemption from taxation.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(1): 53B-21-101 For the purpose of paying all or part of the costs of a project under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(2): The board may, in order to secure the payment of the loan, grant a mortgage, trust deed, or other security device covering all or part of the project, and the land acquired for the project and upon which the project is situated.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(3): The rights and remedies available in the event of a default to the mortgagee, trustee, or other lender are subject to agreement as contained in the mortgage, trust deed, or other security instrument.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(4): The agreement may provide that, in the event of a default in the payment or the violation of any agreement contained in the document, the mortgage, trust deed, or other security instrument may be foreclosed or otherwise realized in any manner permitted by law.  However, no deficiency judgment shall lie in any event and no breach of the agreement shall impose any general obligations or liability upon the state or the borrowing institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(5): The note or other evidence of indebtedness may have all the qualities and incidents of negotiable paper, and is not subject to taxation by the state, except for the corporate franchise tax, or to taxation by any county, municipality, or political subdivision of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(6): The note or other evidence of indebtedness and mortgage may contain additional provisions with respect to repayment out of the income and revenues derived from the operation of the building, from the imposition of student building fees, land grant interest, and net profits from proprietary activities, or from sources other than appropriations by the Legislature to any issuing institution as the board considers necessary and proper.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(7): The board may enter into an agreement it considers necessary with the lending institution as to the use which will be made of any project, the operation, maintenance, and supervision of the project, the imposition of fees, charges, and rentals for its use, including the equipment contained therein, and the collection and disposition to be made of the proceeds of fees, charges, and rentals.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(8): In order to secure the prompt payment of principal and interest and to pay the cost of the maintenance and operation of the project, the board has the same power and authority with respect to the indebtedness created under this section as it has in respect to the issuance of bonds under the other provisions of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(9): When any obligation owing to finance the cost of any project constructed or acquired under this section has been fully paid as to principal and interest, the mortgage is satisfied and discharged.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-111(10): All buildings and additions to existing buildings erected, and the equipment therefor, is exempt from taxation as long as the legal title remains in the borrowing agency.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112 Financing projects and buildings -- Security instruments -- Terms.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112(1): In connection with the financing of any project or building under this chapter, the board, on behalf of an institution of higher education, may grant a purchase money mortgage, trust deed, or other security device pledging any land, buildings, furnishings, equipment, or other facilities to be acquired or constructed and paid for from the proceeds of the financing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112(2): The rights and remedies available in the event of a default to the mortgagee, trustee, or lender shall be as agreed upon between the board and the lender and contained in the document.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112(3): In making any agreements, the board does not have the power to obligate itself or the state, except with respect to: (a) the project; (b) the building and the application of the revenues from it; (c) the revenues from any special fund pledged to repay it; (d) the proceeds of any ad valorem tax; or (e) any appropriations from the Legislature of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112(4): Any purchase money mortgage, trust deed, or other security device made or granted by the board to secure the loan or other method of financing may also provide that in the event of a default in payment or the violation of any agreement, the mortgage, trust deed, or security device may be foreclosed or otherwise realized in any manner permitted by law.  However, no deficiency judgment shall lie in any event and the breach of the agreement does not impose any general obligation or liability upon the board, the state, the proceeds of ad valorem taxes, or appropriations from the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-112(5): The purchase money mortgage, trust deed, or other security device may also provide that any mortgagee, trustee, lender, or the holder of any evidence of indebtedness secured by the security instrument may become the purchaser at any foreclosure sale, if the highest bidder.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-21-113 Limitation on issuance of bonds.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
No bonds may be authorized or issued by the board or the board of any institution under this chapter without the prior approval of the Legislature.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(1): 63A-5b-401 "Capital development" means the same as capital development project, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(2): "Consumer Price Index" means the Consumer Price Index for All Urban Consumers as published by the Bureau of Labor Statistics of the United States Department of Labor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(3): "Dedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from an institution's allocation are requested or used.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(4): 53B-22-202 "Fund" means the Higher Education Capital Projects Fund created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(5): "Institution" means a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(6): 53B-22-203 "Institution's allocation" means the total amount of money in the fund that an institution has been allocated in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(7): "Nondedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from a source other than an institution's allocation are requested or used.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-201(8): 63A-5b-401 "State funds" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-202(2): 53B-22-204; (3) Subject to appropriation, money in the fund shall be used:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-202(2)(a): 53B-22-204 for a dedicated project approved in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-202(2)(b): (3) to pay debt service in accordance with Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-202(3)(b): if the Legislature approves the use by a vote of two-thirds of all members elected to each house.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-202(4): The fund shall be funded by appropriations.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203 Fund money -- Institution allocations.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1): (1)(a); 53B-7-706; (1)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(a): Based on appropriations to the fund, the board shall annually determine how to allocate among all institutions money that has not been previously allocated to an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(b): (1)(a); 53B-7-706 The board shall make the determination described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(b)(i): enrollment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(b)(ii): 53B-7-706 total performance across the metrics described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(b)(iii): projected growth in student population;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-203(1)(b)(iv): existing square feet per student full-time equivalent;

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 23 - Instructional Materials for Students with a Disability Act
*********************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Instructional Materials for Students with a Disability Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
For purposes of this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-106
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1)(a): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-106 "Instructional material or materials" means textbooks and other materials written and published primarily for use by students in postsecondary instruction that are required or essential to a student's success in a course of study in which a student with a disability is enrolled.  The determination of which materials are "required or essential to student success" shall be made by the instructor of the course in consultation with the official making the request pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1)(b): "Instructional material or materials" does not include nontextual mathematics and science materials until the time software becomes commercially available that permits the conversion of existing electronic files of the materials into a format that is compatible with braille translation software or alternative media for students with disabilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(2): "Printed instructional material or materials" means instructional material or materials in book or other printed form.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(3): "Nonprinted instructional materials" means instructional materials in formats other than print, and includes instructional materials that require the availability of electronic equipment in order to be used as a learning resource, including software programs, video disks, and video and audio tapes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(4): 53B-2-101 "State institution of higher education" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(5): "Specialized format" means braille, audio, or digital text that is exclusively for use by blind or other persons with disabilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6)(a): "Structural integrity" means all of the printed instructional material, including the text of the material, sidebars, the table of contents, chapter headings and subheadings, footnotes, indexes, glossaries, and bibliographies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6)(b): "Structural integrity" need not include nontextual elements such as pictures, illustrations, graphs, or charts.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103 Instructional materials to be provided in electronic format.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(a): On or after January 1, 2009, any person that publishes or manufactures printed instructional material for students attending a state institution of higher education shall provide to the institution for use by students attending the institution any printed instructional material in an electronic format mutually agreed upon by the publisher or manufacturer and the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b): Computer files or electronic versions of the printed instructional material shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(i): maintain the structural integrity of the printed instructional material;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(ii): be compatible with commonly used braille translation and speech synthesis software; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(iii): include corrections and revisions as may be necessary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(c): (1)(a) If good faith efforts fail to produce an agreement pursuant to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2): The computer files or electronic versions of the printed instructional material shall be provided to the institution at no additional cost and in a timely manner, upon receipt of a written request that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(a): certifies that the institution has purchased the printed instructional material for use by a student with a disability or that a student with a disability attending or registered to attend that institution has purchased the printed instructional material;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(b): certifies that the student has a disability that prevents the student from using standard instructional materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(c): certifies that the printed instructional material is for use by the student in connection with a course in which the student is registered or enrolled at the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(d): is signed by the coordinator of services for students with disabilities at the institution or by the official responsible for monitoring compliance with the Americans with Disabilities Act of 1990, 42 U.S.C. 12101 et seq. at the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3): (2)(a); (2)(d) A publisher or manufacturer providing instructional materials in an electronic format to an institution may require that, in addition to the requirements specified in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3)(a): the student will use the electronic copy of the printed instructional material in specialized format solely for the student's own educational purposes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3)(b): the student will not copy or duplicate the printed instructional material for use by others.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(4): If an institution permits a student to directly use the electronic version of an instructional material, the disk or file shall be copy-protected or the institution shall take other reasonable precautions to ensure that the student does not copy or distribute electronic versions of instructional materials in violation of the Copyright Revisions Act of 1976, 17 U.S.C. Sec. 101 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(5): (1); (2) A person that publishes or manufactures nonprinted instructional materials for students attending a state institution of higher education shall provide computer files or other electronic versions of the nonprinted instructional materials for use by students attending the institution subject to the same requirements specified in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(6): Nothing in this chapter shall be construed to prohibit an institution from assisting a student with a disability by using the electronic version of printed instructional material provided pursuant to this section solely to transcribe or arrange for the transcription of the printed instructional materials into braille.  If a transcription is made, the institution shall have the right to share the braille copy of the printed instructional material with other students with disabilities.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104 Centers for processing requests for electronic versions of instructional materials.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(1): The board may establish one or more centers to process requests for electronic versions of instructional materials pursuant to this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(2): The institutions designated as within the jurisdiction of a center shall submit requests for instructional material to the center, which shall transmit the request to the publisher or manufacturer.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(3): If there is more than one center, each center shall make every effort to coordinate requests.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(4): The publisher or manufacturer of instructional material shall be required to honor and respond to only those requests submitted through a designated center.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(5): If a publisher or manufacturer has responded to a request for instructional materials by a center, all subsequent requests for those instructional materials shall be satisfied by the center to which the request is made.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-105 Infringement of copyright laws not authorized.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Nothing in this chapter shall be considered to authorize any use of instructional materials that would constitute an infringement of copyright under the Copyright Revision Act of 1976, as amended, 17 U.S.C. Sec. 101 et seq.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106 Board to make rules.
-----------------------------------------------------
In accordance withUtah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(1): the designation of materials considered "required or essential to student success";
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(2): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-102 the determination of the availability of technology for the conversion of nonprinted materials pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(3): 53B-23-103 the procedures and standards relating to distribution of files and materials pursuant to Section


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 25 - Internet Postsecondary Institution Privacy Act
*********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Internet Postsecondary Institution Privacy Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1)(a): "Personal Internet account" means an online account that is used by a student or prospective student exclusively for personal communications unrelated to any purpose of the postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1)(b): "Personal Internet account" does not include an account created, maintained, used, or accessed by a student or prospective student for education related communications or for an educational purpose of the postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(2): "Postsecondary institution" means an institution that provides educational services offered primarily to persons who have completed or terminated their secondary or high school education or who are beyond the age of compulsory school attendance.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201 Prohibited activities.
-------------------------------------------------------
A postsecondary institution may not do any of the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201(1): request a student or prospective student to disclose a username and password, or a password that allows access to the student's or prospective student's personal Internet account; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201(2): (1) expel, discipline, fail to admit, or otherwise penalize a student or prospective student for failure to disclose information specified in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202 Permitted activities.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1): This chapter does not prohibit a postsecondary institution from requesting or requiring a student to disclose a username or password to gain access to or operate the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1)(a): an electronic communications device supplied by or paid for in whole or in part by the postsecondary institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1)(b): an account or service provided by the postsecondary institution that is either obtained by virtue of the student's admission to the postsecondary institution or used by the student for educational purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(2): 53B-25-201(1) This chapter does not prohibit or restrict a postsecondary institution from viewing, accessing, or using information about a student or prospective student that can be obtained without the information described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203 Duties not created.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203(1): This chapter does not create a duty for a postsecondary institution to search or monitor the activity of a personal Internet account.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203(2): A postsecondary institution is not liable under this chapter for failure to request or require that a student or prospective student grant access to, allow observation of, or disclose information that allows access to or observation of the student's or prospective student's personal Internet account.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301 Private right of action.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301(1): A person aggrieved by a violation of this chapter may bring a civil cause of action against a postsecondary institution in a court of competent jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301(2): (1) In an action brought under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(1): 53B-26-303 "Advisory council" means the Deep Technology Talent Advisory Council created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(a): "Deep technology" means technology that leads to new products and innovations based on scientific discovery or meaningful engineering innovation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b): "Deep technology" may include technology that leads to new products and innovations related to one or more of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(i): advanced materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(ii): artificial intelligence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(iii): augmented and virtual reality;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(iv): biotechnology;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(v): photonics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(vi): quantum computing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(vii): robotics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(viii): secure computing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(2)(b)(ix): other emerging technologies as determined by the advisory council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-301(3): "Institution of higher education" means the University of Utah, Utah State University, Southern Utah University, Weber State University, Snow College, Utah Tech University, Utah Valley University, or Salt Lake Community College.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302 Deep technology initiative.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(1): Subject to appropriations from the Legislature and in accordance with the proposal process and other provisions of this section, the board shall develop and oversee a deep technology talent initiative that includes providing funding for expanded programs in deep technology.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(2): The board shall facilitate collaborations that create expanded, multidisciplinary programs or stackable credential programs in both undergraduate and graduate studies that prepare students to be workforce participants in jobs requiring deep technology skills.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3): An institution of higher education seeking to partner with one or more participating employers shall submit a proposal to the board, in a form approved by the board and in accordance with deadlines determined by the board, which contains the following elements:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(a): a description of the proposed program in deep technology that demonstrates the program will:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(a)(i): be responsive to the deep technology talent needs of the state through industry involvement in the project's design;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(a)(ii): be a partnership that includes at least one participating employer and at least one institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(a)(iii): address a previously unmet state need related to deep technology;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(b): an estimate of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(b)(i): student enrollment in the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(b)(ii): what academic credit or credentials will be provided by the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(b)(iii): occupations for which graduates will be qualified;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(c): evidence that each participating employer is committed to participating and contributing to the program by providing any combination of instruction, extensive workplace experience, or mentoring;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(d): a description of any resources that will be provided by each participating employer in the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(3)(e): the amount of funding requested for the program, including justification for the funding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4): (3) The board shall provide all proposals to the advisory council and the advisory council shall review and prioritize each proposal received and recommend to the board whether the proposal should be funded, including the recommended amount of funding, using the following criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(a): (3) the quality and completeness of the elements of the proposal described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b): to what extent the proposed program:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(i): would expand the capacity to meet state or regional workforce needs related to deep technology;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(ii): would integrate deep technology competency with disciplinary expertise;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(iii): identifies a faculty member or other individual who has expertise and a demonstrated willingness to lead the proposed program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(iv): would incorporate internships or significant project experiences, including team-based experiences;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(v): identifies how industry professionals would participate in curriculum development and teaching;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(vi): would create partnerships with other higher education institutions and industry; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(b)(vii): would be cost effective; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(4)(c): other relevant criteria as determined by the advisory council and the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-26-302(5): (6); (4) Subject to Subsection

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 27 - Campus Individual Rights Act
***************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101(1): This chapter is known as the "Campus Individual Rights Act."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101(2): This part is known as "General Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "institution" means an institution of higher education listed in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-201 Title.
---------------------------------------
This part is known as the "Campus Free Expression Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "expressive activity" includes:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(1): peacefully assembling, protesting, or speaking;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(2): distributing literature;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(3): carrying a sign; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(4): circulating a petition.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203 Expressive activities at an institution.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(1): An outdoor area of an institution's campus is a traditional public forum.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2): An institution may maintain and enforce reasonable time, place, or manner restrictions on an expressive activity in an outdoor area of the institution's campus, if the restrictions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(a): are narrowly tailored to serve a significant institutional interest;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(b): are based on published, content-neutral, and viewpoint-neutral criteria; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(c): leave open ample alternative channels for communication.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3): (2) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3)(a): a member of the institution's community or the public from spontaneously and contemporaneously assembling in an outdoor area of the institution's campus; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3)(b): a person from freely engaging in noncommercial expressive activity in an outdoor area of the institution's campus if the person's conduct is lawful.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(4): This part does not apply to expressive activity in an area on an institution's campus other than an outdoor area.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204 Cause of action.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1): The following persons may bring an action in a state court of competent jurisdiction to enjoin a violation of this part or to recover compensatory damages, reasonable court costs, or reasonable attorney fees:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1)(a): the attorney general; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1)(b): a person claiming that the person's expressive rights, as described in this part, were violated.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2): In an action brought under this part, if the court finds a violation of this part, the court:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(a): shall enjoin the violation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b): shall, if a person whose expressive rights were violated brought the action, award the person:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b)(i): at least $500 for an initial violation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b)(ii): if the person notifies the institution of the violation, $50 for each day the violation continues after the notification; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c): may award a prevailing plaintiff:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(i): compensatory damages;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(ii): reasonable court costs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(iii): reasonable attorney fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(3): Title 63G, Chapter 7, Governmental Immunity Act of Utah Notwithstanding


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205 Statute of limitations.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(1): (3) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(2): Each day that a violation continues after an initial violation, and each day that an institution's policy in violation of this part remains in effect, shall constitute a continuing violation of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(3): (2); (1) For a continuing violation described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301(1): "Civil liberty" means a civil liberty enumerated in the United States Constitution or the Utah Constitution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301(2): 63G-3-601 "Initiate rulemaking proceedings" means the same as that term is defined in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302 Policies requiring rulemaking -- Policy review.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act An institution may not make or amend a policy that directly affects a student's civil liberty, unless the policy is made a rule in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2): (2)(a) Each institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2)(a): before November 30, 2018, review the institution's policies as of May 11, 2018, and identify any policy that directly affects a student's civil liberty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2)(b): (2)(a) before August 1, 2019, for each policy identified under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303 Complaint process -- Reporting.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act Before August 1, 2019, the board shall make rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2): (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a): (1) When a student submits a complaint in accordance with the rules adopted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(i): examine the complaint and, within 30 days after the day on which the board receives the complaint, determine whether the complaint is made in good faith; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii)(A): if the board determines that the complaint is made in good faith, direct the institution against which the complaint is made to initiate rulemaking proceedings for the challenged policy; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii)(B): if the board determines that the complaint is made in bad faith, dismiss the complaint.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b): Before November 30 of each year, the board shall submit a report to the Administrative Rules Review and General Oversight Committee detailing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(i): the number of complaints the board received during the preceding year;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(ii): the number of complaints the board found to be made in good faith during the preceding year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(iii): each policy that is the subject of a good-faith complaint that the board received during the preceding year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(3): If the board directs an institution to initiate rulemaking proceedings for a challenged policy in accordance with this section, the institution shall initiate rulemaking proceedings for the policy within 60 days after the day on which the board directs the institution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1): "Discriminatory harassment" means student-on-student speech that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(a): is unwelcome;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(b): discriminates on the basis of a classification protected under federal or state law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(c): is so severe, pervasive, and objectively offensive, and that so undermines and distracts from a student's educational experience, that the student is effectively denied access to an institution's resource or opportunity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(2): "Student" means an individual enrolled at an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a): "Student-on-student speech" means verbal, written, or other communication that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a)(i): communicated by a student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a)(ii): directed at another student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(b): "Student-on-student speech" does not include an act of physical contact between a student and another student.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402 Institution duties.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1): An institution is in violation of this part if the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1)(a): gains actual knowledge of discriminatory harassment in the institution's program or activity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1)(b): acts with deliberate indifference to the discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2)(a): An institution may not sanction or discipline, as discriminatory harassment, student-on-student speech that does not constitute discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2)(b): An institution is not liable under this part for failing to sanction or discipline a student who communicates student-on-student speech that is not discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(3): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from sanctioning or disciplining student-on-student speech that is otherwise not protected under the First Amendment to the United States Constitution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(4): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from responding to student-on-student speech that is not discriminatory harassment by taking nonpunitive actions designed to promote a welcoming, inclusive environment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(5): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from maintaining policies prohibiting stalking or other criminal activity.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-403 Cause of action.
-------------------------------------------------
The attorney general may bring an action to enjoin a violation of this part, in a state court of competent jurisdiction, against an institution or an institution's agent acting in the agent's official capacity.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404 Statute of limitations.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(1): (3)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(2): 53B-27-402(2)(a); 53B-27-402(2)(a) For an action alleging a violation of Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(3)(a): 53B-27-402(1) For an action alleging a violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(3)(b): (3)(a); (1) For an action described in Subsection
