Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501 Free expression policies.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(1): As used in this section, "free expression policy" means an institution's policy, regulation, or other expectation related to student expression.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a): publish the institution's free expression policies:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a)(i): in the institution's student handbook; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a)(ii): on the institution's website;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(b): include information about the institution's free expression policies in an orientation program for students enrolled in the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(c): develop a program, procedures, and materials to ensure that an individual who has responsibility for the discipline or education of a student at the institution understands the institution's free expression policies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3): (2)(c) An individual described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(a): administrator;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(b): campus police officer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(c): residence life official; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(d): faculty member.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(4): An institution shall ensure that a free expression policy is consistent with the provisions of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 28 - Student Rights and Responsibilities
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Student Rights and Responsibilities."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "institution" means a public or private postsecondary institution that is located in Utah, including an institution of higher education listed in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1): "Certified advocate" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(a): is employed by or volunteers at a qualified institutional victim services provider;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(b): has completed at least 40 hours of training in counseling and assisting victims of sexual harassment, sexual assault, rape, dating violence, domestic violence, or stalking; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(c): acts under the supervision of the director or director's designee of a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a): "Confidential communication" means information that is communicated by a victim, in the course of the victim seeking an institutional advocacy service, to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(i): a certified advocate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(ii): a qualified institutional victim services provider;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(iii): a person reasonably necessary for the transmission of the information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(iv): an individual who is present at the time the information is transmitted for the purpose of furthering the victim's interests; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(v): another individual, in the context of group counseling at a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(b): (2)(a) "Confidential communication" includes a record that is created or maintained as a result of the communication described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3): "Institutional advocacy service" means a safety planning, counseling, psychological, support, advocacy, medical, or legal service that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a): addresses issues involving:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(i): sexual harassment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(ii): sexual assault;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(iii): rape;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(iv): domestic violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(v): dating violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(vi): stalking; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(b): is provided by a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a): "Qualified institutional victim services provider" means an organization that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(i): is affiliated with an institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(ii): employs or provides volunteer opportunities for certified advocates;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(iii): provides an institutional advocacy service to victims or families of victims; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(iv): is designated by the affiliated institution as a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b): "Qualified institutional victim services provider" may include an institution's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(i): sexual assault center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(ii): victim advocacy center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(iii): women's center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(iv): health center; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(v): counseling service center.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(5): "Record" means a book, letter, document, paper, map, plan, photograph, film, card, tape, recording, electronic data, or other documentary material regardless of physical form or characteristics.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(6): "Victim" means an individual who seeks an institutional advocacy service.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202 Confidentiality of information -- Disclosure of confidential communication.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(1): (2); Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(2): 26B-6-205; 80-2-602; 78B-3-502 A person may disclose a confidential communication if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(2)(a): the victim gives written and informed consent to the disclosure;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(2)(b): 26B-6-205; 80-2-602; 78B-3-502 the person has an obligation to disclose the confidential communication under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(2)(c): the disclosure is required by federal law; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-202(2)(d): a court of competent jurisdiction orders the disclosure.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(1): "Alleged perpetrator" means an individual whom a victim alleges committed an act of sexual violence against the victim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(2): "Code of conduct" means an institution's student code of conduct, student code of ethics, honor code, or other policy under which the institution may sanction a student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(3): "Covered allegation" means an allegation made to an institution that an individual committed an act of sexual violence.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(4): "Law enforcement agency" means an off-campus law enforcement agency of the unit of local government with jurisdiction to respond to a covered allegation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5): "Sexual violence" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(a): sexual abuse as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 2242;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(b): aggravated sexual abuse as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 2241;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(c): assault resulting in substantial bodily injury as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 113(a)(7);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(d): sexual assault;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(e): dating violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(f): domestic violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(g): stalking.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(6): "Student" means an individual enrolled in an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(7): "Victim" means a student who alleges that the student was a victim of sexual violence.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302 Code of conduct violation -- Report of sexual violence.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
An institution may not sanction a student for a code of conduct violation related to the use of drugs or alcohol if:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1): the student is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1)(a): a victim of an act of sexual violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1)(b): a witness to an act of sexual violence;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303 Institution engagement with a law enforcement agency -- Articulable and significant threat -- Notification to victim.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(1): (1)(a); (1)(a); (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(1)(a): An institution shall keep confidential from a law enforcement agency a covered allegation reported to the institution by the victim of the covered allegation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(1)(b): (1)(a); (1)(a); (2) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(1)(b)(i): if the victim consents to the institution engaging with the law enforcement agency; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(1)(b)(ii): (2) in accordance with Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(a): (3); (1)(a); (2)(b) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b): (2)(a) To determine whether the information in a covered allegation creates an articulable and significant threat described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(i): whether the circumstances of the covered allegation suggest an increased risk that the alleged perpetrator will commit an additional act of sexual violence or other violence;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(iv): whether the alleged perpetrator is alleged to have threatened further sexual violence or other violence against the victim or another individual;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(v): whether the act of sexual violence was committed by more than one alleged perpetrator;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(vi): whether the circumstances of the covered allegation suggest there is an increased risk of future acts of sexual violence under similar circumstances;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(vii): whether the act of sexual violence was perpetrated with a weapon; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-303(2)(b)(viii): the age of the victim.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(2)(a): upon a victim of or a witness to an act of sexual violence alleged in a covered allegation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(2)(b): in retaliation for the victim's or the witness's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(2)(b)(i): report of the covered allegation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(2)(b)(ii): involvement in an investigation initiated by the institution in response to the covered allegation.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a): communicates an intention to inflict bodily injury:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a)(i): upon a victim of or a witness to an act of sexual violence alleged in a covered allegation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a)(ii): in retaliation for the victim's or the witness's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a)(ii)(A): report of the covered allegation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a)(ii)(B): involvement in an investigation initiated by the institution in response to the covered allegation; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a): study issues related to providing public safety services on institution campuses, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(i): policies and practices for hiring, supervision, and firing of campus law enforcement officers;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(v): roles, responsibilities, jurisdiction, and authority of local law enforcement and campus law enforcement, including authority based on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(v)(A): the type of public safety services provided; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(v)(B): geographic boundaries;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(vi): how an institution and local law enforcement coordinate to respond to on-campus and off-campus incidents requiring public safety services, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(vi)(A): legal requirements or restrictions affecting coordination;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(vi)(B): agreements, practices, or procedures governing coordination between an institution and local law enforcement, including mutual support, sharing information, or dispatch management; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(vi)(C): any issues that may affect the timeliness of a response to an on-campus or off-campus incident reported by or involving a student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(vii): infrastructure, staffing, and equipment considerations that impact the effectiveness of campus law enforcement or local law enforcement responses to an on-campus or off-campus incident reported by or involving a student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(viii): the benefits and disadvantages of an institution employing campus law enforcement compared to local law enforcement providing public safety services on an institution campus;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(ix): an institution's compliance with federal and state crime statistic reporting requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(x): how an institution informs faculty, staff, and students about a crime or emergency on campus;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(xi): national best practices for providing public safety services on institution campuses, including differences in best practices based on the size, infrastructure, location, and other relevant characteristics of a college or university; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(a)(xii): any other issue the board determines is relevant to the study;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(b): make recommendations for providing public safety services on institution campuses statewide;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(c): (2)(b) produce a final report of the study described in this section, including the recommendations described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-402(2)(d): 68-3-14; (2)(c) in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(ii): (1)(d)(i) "Institution noncampus housing facility" includes real property that is adjacent to, and is used in direct support of, the building or property described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(i)(B): part of the institution's campus.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(1): 53B-28-502 "Advisory group" means the institution of higher education privacy advisory group established by the state privacy officer under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(2): "Aggregate data" means data that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(2)(a): are totaled and reported at the group, cohort, class, course, institution, region, or state level, with at least 10 individuals in the level; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(2)(b): do not reveal personally identifiable student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(3): "Data breach" means an unauthorized release of or unauthorized access to personally identifiable student data that an education entity maintains.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4): "Data governance plan" means an education entity's comprehensive plan for managing education data that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(a): incorporates reasonable data industry best practices to maintain and protect student data and other education-related data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(b): describes the role, responsibility, and authority of the board or an institution privacy officer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(c): provides for necessary technical assistance, training, support, and auditing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(d): describes the process for sharing student data between the education entity and another person;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(e): describes the education entity's data expungement process, including how to respond to requests for expungement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(f): describes the data breach response process; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(4)(g): is published annually and available on the institution's website or the Utah System of Higher Education's website.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(5): "Education entity" means the Utah Board of Higher Education or an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(6): 53B-28-503 "Higher education privacy officer" means a privacy officer that the board designates under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(7): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(8): "Minor" means a person younger than 18 years old.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(a): "Personally identifiable student data" means student data that identifies or is used by the holder to identify a student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b): "Personally identifiable student data" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(i): a student's first and last name;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(ii): the first and last name of a student's family member;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(iii): a student's or a student's family's home or physical address;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(iv): a student's email address or other online contact information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(v): a student's telephone number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(vi): a student's social security number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(vii): a student's biometric identifier;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(viii): a student's health or disability data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(ix): a student's education entity student identification number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(x): a student's social media user name and password or alias;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xi): if associated with personally identifiable student data, the student's persistent identifier, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xi)(A): a customer number held in a cookie; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xi)(B): a processor serial number;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xii): a combination of a student's last name or photograph with other information that together permits a person to contact the student online;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xiii): information about a student or a student's family that a person collects online and combines with other personally identifiable student data to identify the student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(9)(b)(xiv): information that, alone or in combination, is linked or linkable to a specific student that would allow a reasonable person in the school community, who does not have personal knowledge of the relevant circumstances, to identify the student with reasonable certainty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(10): 67-3-13 "State privacy officer" means the state privacy officer described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(11): "Student" means an individual enrolled in an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(12): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(12)(a): "Student data" means information about a student at the individual student level.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(12)(b): "Student data" does not include aggregate or de-identified data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(13): "Third-party contractor" means a person who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(13)(a): is not an institution or an employee of an institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-501(13)(b): pursuant to a contract with an education entity, collects or receives student data in order to provide a product or service, as described in the contract, if the product or service is not related to school photography, yearbooks, graduation announcements, or a similar product or service.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502 State student data protection governance.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502(1): The state privacy officer shall establish a higher education privacy advisory group to advise institutions and institution boards of trustees on student data protection.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502(2): The advisory group shall consist of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502(2)(a): the state privacy officer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502(2)(b): the higher education privacy officer; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-502(3)(a)(i)(B): board policies of the Utah Board of Higher Education or institutions; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505 Third-party contractors.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(1): A third-party contractor shall use personally identifiable student data received under a contract with an education entity strictly for the purpose of providing the contracted product or service within the negotiated contract terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2): 53B-28-502(5); (4) When contracting with a third-party contractor on or after January 1, 2024, an education entity, or a government agency contracting on behalf of an education entity, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(a): 53B-28-502(5) ensure that the contract terms comply with the standards the board establishes under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b): (4) require the following provisions in the contract:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b)(i): requirements and restrictions related to the collection, use, storage, or sharing of student data by the third-party contractor that are necessary for the education entity to ensure compliance with the provisions of this part and board rule;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b)(ii): a description of a person, or type of person, including an affiliate of the third-party contractor, with whom the third-party contractor may share student data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b)(iii): provisions that, at the request of the education entity, govern the deletion of the student data received by the third-party contractor;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b)(iv): (4) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(2)(b)(v): an agreement by the third-party contractor that, at the request of the education entity that is a party to the contract, the education entity or the education entity's designee may audit the third-party contractor to verify compliance with the contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(3): As authorized by law or court order, a third-party contractor shall share student data as requested by law enforcement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4): A third-party contractor may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(a): use student data for adaptive learning or customized student learning purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(b): market an educational application or product to a student if the third-party contractor does not use student data, shared by or collected on behalf of an education entity, to market the educational application or product;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(c): use a recommendation engine to recommend to a student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(c)(i): content that relates to learning or employment, within the third-party contractor's application, if the recommendation is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(c)(ii): services that relate to learning or employment, within the third-party contractor's application, if the recommendation is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(d): respond to a student request for information or feedback, if the content of the response is not motivated by payment or other consideration from another party;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(e): use student data to allow or improve operability and functionality of the third-party contractor's application; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(f): identify for a student nonprofit institutions of higher education or scholarship providers that are seeking students who meet specific criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(f)(i): regardless of whether the identified nonprofit institutions of higher education or scholarship providers provide payment or other consideration to the third-party contractor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(f)(ii): only if the third-party contractor obtains authorization in writing from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(f)(ii)(A): the student's parent, if the student is a minor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(4)(f)(ii)(B): the student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(5): At the completion of a contract with an education entity, if the contract has not been renewed, a third-party contractor shall return or delete upon the education entity's request all personally identifiable student data under the control of the education entity unless a student or a minor student's parent consents to the maintenance of the personally identifiable student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6): (6)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6)(a): (6)(b) A third-party contractor may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6)(a)(i): (6)(b) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6)(a)(ii): collect, use, or share student data, if the collection, use, or sharing of the student data is inconsistent with the third-party contractor's contract with the education entity; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6)(a)(iii): use student data for targeted advertising.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(6)(b): A person may obtain student data through the purchase of, merger with, or otherwise acquiring a third-party contractor if the third-party contractor remains in compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(7): The provisions of this section do not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(7)(a): apply to the use of a general audience application, including the access of a general audience application with login credentials created by a third-party contractor's application;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(7)(b): apply if the student data is shared in accordance with the education entity's directory information policy, as described in 34 C.F.R. Sec. 99.37;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(7)(c): apply to the providing of Internet service; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(7)(d): impose a duty on a provider of an interactive computer service, as defined in 47 U.S.C. Sec. 230, to review or enforce compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(8): A provision of this section that relates to a student's student data does not apply to a third-party contractor if the education entity or third-party contractor obtains authorization from the following individual, in writing, to waive that provision:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(8)(a): the student's parent, if the student is a minor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-505(8)(b): the student.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506 Penalties.
-------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1): (1)(d); (1)(b) A third-party contractor that knowingly or recklessly permits unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data under this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(a): (1)(d) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(b): may be required by the board to pay a civil penalty of up to $25,000.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(c): may be required to pay:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(c)(i): an institution's cost of notifying parents and students of the unauthorized sharing or use of student data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(c)(ii): any expense incurred by the institution as result of the unauthorized sharing or use of student data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(d): An education entity may enter into a contract with a third-party contractor that knowingly or recklessly permitted unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(d)(i): the education entity determines that the third-party contractor has corrected the errors that caused the unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(d)(ii): the third-party contractor demonstrates:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(d)(ii)(A): if the third-party contractor is under contract with the education entity, current compliance with this part; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(d)(ii)(B): an ability to comply with the requirements of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(e): (1)(b) The board may bring an action in the district court of the county in which the office of the education entity is located, if necessary, to enforce payment of the civil penalty described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(1)(f): An individual who knowingly or intentionally permits unauthorized collecting, sharing, or use of student data may be found guilty of a class A misdemeanor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(2): 53B-28-505; 53B-28-505
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(2)(a): 53B-28-505 A student or a minor student's parent may bring an action against a third-party contractor in a court of competent jurisdiction for damages caused by a knowing or reckless violation of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(2)(b): 53B-28-505 If the court finds that a third-party contractor has violated Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(2)(b)(i): damages; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-506(2)(b)(ii): costs.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 29 - Utah Valley University
*********************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Utah Valley University."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-201(1): 53B-29-202 "Fire and rescue training program" means the program described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-201(2): 53-7-203 "Fire board" means the Utah Fire Prevention Board, created in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202 Fire prevention, education, and training program.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1): With technical advice and support from the fire board, Utah Valley University shall operate a statewide fire and rescue service training program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(a): provides instruction, training, and testing for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(a)(i): Utah Valley University students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(a)(ii): firefighters and emergency rescue personnel throughout the state, whether paid or volunteer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(b): explores new methods of firefighting, fire training, and fire prevention;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(c): provides training for fire and arson detection and investigation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(d): provides training to students, firefighters, and emergency rescue personnel on how to conduct public education programs to promote fire safety;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(e): provides for certification of firefighters, pump operators, instructors, officers, and rescue personnel; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(1)(f): provides facilities and props for teaching firefighting and emergency rescue skills.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(2): Utah Valley University shall ensure that the curriculum, training, and facilities offered in the fire and rescue training program are sufficient to allow individuals who successfully complete the program to receive applicable certification as a firefighter or emergency rescue professional.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(3): Utah Valley University and the fire board shall consult together regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(3)(a): the development and content of the curriculum and training of the fire and rescue training program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(3)(b): the identification of individuals who will be permitted to participate in the fire and rescue program without cost; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(3)(c): the establishment of certification standards and requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(4): Utah Valley University shall allow individuals designated by the fire board to participate in and complete the fire and rescue training program without cost and to receive applicable certification.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(5): Utah Valley University and the fire board shall by contract establish terms to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(5)(a): define the scope and content of the fire and rescue training program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(5)(b): identify the fire and rescue personnel throughout the state who will be permitted to participate in the fire and rescue training program without cost; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-202(5)(c): define other aspects of the relationship between Utah Valley University and the fire board relating to the fire and rescue training program that are mutually beneficial.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-203 Reporting requirement.
-------------------------------------------------------
In 2023, no later than October 31, 2023, Utah Valley University and the fire board shall report to the Education Interim Committee, the Law Enforcement and Criminal Justice Interim Committee, and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee of the Legislature about:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-203(1): the operation of the fire and rescue training program, including successes and challenges associated with the operation of the fire and rescue training program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-203(2): the positive aspects of and any concerns relating to the relationship between Utah Valley University and the fire board with respect to the fire and rescue training program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-301(1): 53B-29-302 "Initiative" means the Civic Thought and Leadership Initiative described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-301(2): "University" means Utah Valley University.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302 Civic Thought and Leadership Initiative.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302(1): The university shall establish the Civic Thought and Leadership Initiative within the Center for Constitutional Studies to facilitate nonpartisan political discussion and provide civic education and research.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302(2): The initiative shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302(2)(a): provide courses in and related to philosophy, history, economics, and political science;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302(2)(b): provide resources to students, outside academic institutions, government agencies, and other persons regarding civic affairs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-302(2)(c): foster thoughtful civic engagement in Utah and the surrounding region.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-29-303 Acceptance of gifts.
-----------------------------------------------------
The university is authorized to receive gifts, contributions, and donations of all kinds, for development or support of the initiative.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203 Rocky Mountain Center for Occupational and Environmental Health.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(1): There is established at the University of Utah and Weber State University the Rocky Mountain Center for Occupational and Environmental Health, to be a center for occupational health, safety, and environment education and research.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2): (2)(a)(i) The University of Utah and Weber State University shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2)(a): jointly operate the center in a manner so that the center is:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2)(a)(ii): a resource for affected populations to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2)(a)(ii)(A): improve workplace health, safety, and environment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2)(a)(ii)(B): contribute to economic growth and development in Utah and the surrounding region; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(2)(b): (2)(a)(i) each appoint a co-principal investigator upon application for the designation described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-30-203(3): The University of Utah senior vice president for health sciences and the Weber State University provost and vice president of academic affairs shall jointly develop an annual budget for the center that considers funding from all available sources.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 31 - Utah Tech University
*******************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as " Utah Tech University."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-201 Nonprofit corporations or foundations -- Purpose.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-201(1): Utah Tech University may form a nonprofit corporation or foundation controlled by the president of the university and the board to aid and assist the university in attaining its charitable, communications, and other related educational objectives, including support for media innovation, film festivals, film production, print media, broadcasting, television, and digital media.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-201(2): The nonprofit corporation or foundation may receive and administer legislative appropriations, government grants, contracts, and private gifts to carry out its public purposes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301 Utah Tech University Higher Education for Incarcerated Youth Program.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(a): "Interactive video conferencing" means two-way, real-time transmission of audio and video signals between devices or computers at two or more locations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(b): "Program" means the Utah Tech University Higher Education for Incarcerated Youth Program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(c): "Student" means an individual who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(c)(i): in the custody of the Division of Juvenile Justice and Youth Services at any time a course is being offered, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(c)(i)(A): individuals in the legal custody of the Division of Juvenile Justice and Youth Services; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(c)(i)(B): individuals who are housed in a detention center that the Division of Juvenile Justice and Youth Services operates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(1)(c)(ii): subject to the jurisdiction of the Youth Parole Authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2): Consistent with policies established by the board, Utah Tech University shall, subject to legislative appropriation, establish and administer the Utah Tech University Higher Education for Incarcerated Youth Program to provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(a): students needing high school credits opportunities for concurrent enrollment courses;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(b): a consistent, two-year, flexible schedule of higher education courses delivered through interactive video conferencing, in-person, or online methods to students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(c): a pathway for students to earn college credits that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(c)(i): apply toward earning a certificate, associate degree, bachelor's degree; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(c)(ii): satisfy scholarship requirements or other objectives that best meet the needs of an individual student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-301(2)(d): advisory support to students and academic counselors who participate in the program to ensure that the students' higher education courses align with the academic and career goals defined in the students' plans for college and career readiness.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-401 Heritage Committee.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-401(1): The board of trustees shall establish a Heritage Committee to identify and implement strategies to preserve the heritage, culture, and history of the region on the campus of Utah Tech University, including the regional significance of the term "Dixie."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-31-401(2): (1) At or before the November interim meeting in 2022, the board of trustees shall report to the Education Interim Committee regarding the establishment of the Heritage Committee described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 34 - Talent, Education, and Industry Alignment
****************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1): "Apprenticeship program" means a program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(a): combines paid on-the-job learning with formal classroom instruction to prepare students for careers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(b): includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(b)(i): structured on-the-job learning for students under the supervision of a skilled employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(b)(ii): classroom instruction for students related to the on-the-job learning;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(b)(iii): ongoing student assessments using established competency and skills standards; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(1)(b)(iv): the student receiving an industry-recognized credential or degree upon completion of the program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(2): 35A-2-101 "Career and technical education region" means an economic service area created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(3): 63N-1a-201 "Commission" means the Unified Economic Opportunity Commission created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(4): 53G-11-303 "High quality professional learning" means the professional learning standards for teachers and principals described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(5): "Institution of higher education" means the University of Utah, Utah State University, Southern Utah University, Weber State University, Snow College, Utah Tech University, Utah Valley University, or Salt Lake Community College.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(6): "Local education agency" means a school district, a charter school, or the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(7): 53B-34-105 "Master plan" means the computer science education master plan described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(8): "Participating employer" means an employer that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(8)(a): partners with an educational institution on a curriculum for an apprenticeship program or work-based learning program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(8)(b): provides an apprenticeship or work-based learning program for students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(9): "State board" means the State Board of Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(10): 53B-34-102 "Talent board" means the Talent, Education, and Industry Alignment Board created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(11): 53B-34-103 "Talent program" means the Talent Ready Utah Program created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(12): "Targeted industry" means an industry or group of industries targeted by the commission for economic development in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(13): 53B-1-101.5; 53B-2a-201 "Technical college" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(13)(a): 53B-1-101.5 the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(13)(b): 53B-2a-201 a degree-granting institution acting in the degree-granting institution's technical education role described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14)(a): "Work-based learning program" means a program that combines structured and supervised learning activities with authentic work experiences and that is implemented through industry and education partnerships.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14)(b): "Work-based learning program" includes the following objectives:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14)(b)(i): providing students an applied workplace experience using knowledge and skills attained in a program of study that includes an internship, externship, or work experience;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14)(b)(ii): providing an educational institution with objective input from a participating employer regarding the education requirements of the current workforce; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(14)(b)(iii): providing funding for programs that are associated with high-wage, in-demand, or emerging occupations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-101(15): "Workforce programs" means education or industry programs that facilitate training the state's workforce to meet industry demand.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-102 Talent, Education, and Industry Alignment Board -- Creation -- Membership -- Expenses -- Duties.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-102(1): There is created the Talent, Education, and Industry Alignment Board composed of the following members:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-102(1)(a): the state superintendent of public instruction or the superintendent's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-102(1)(b): the commissioner or the commissioner's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-102(1)(c): the chair of the State Board of Education or the chair's designee;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103 Talent Ready Utah Program.
-----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(1): There is created the Talent Ready Utah Program administered by the commissioner.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(2): The commissioner, with the approval of the board, shall appoint a director of the talent program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(3): (5) The director of the talent program:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(3)(a): (5) shall appoint, with the approval of the commissioner, an apprenticeship intermediary, to carry out the duties described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(3)(b): may appoint other staff with the approval of the commissioner.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4): The talent program shall coordinate with the talent board to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(a): further education and industry alignment in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(b): coordinate the development of new education programs that align with industry demand;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(c): coordinate or partner with other state agencies to administer grant programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(d): promote the inclusion of industry partners in education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(e): provide outreach and information to employers regarding workforce programs and initiatives;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(f): develop and analyze stackable credential programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(g): determine efficiencies among workforce providers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(h): map available workforce programs focusing on programs that successfully create high-paying jobs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(4)(i): support initiatives of the talent board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5): (3) The apprenticeship intermediary appointed by the director under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(a): increasing awareness for the talent program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(b): recruiting industry partners;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(c): connecting high school students to participating employers, apprenticeship opportunities, and work-based learning opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(d): working with local education agencies to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(d)(i): integrate talent program apprenticeship opportunities and work-based learning opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(d)(ii): connect high school students with higher education opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(e): training mentors at participating employers in vocational education practices for youth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(f): holding meetings with education partners and industry partners to discuss curriculum needs and industry needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(g): working with institutions of higher education and local education agencies to ensure industry-recognized credential programs are fully stackable; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-103(5)(h): performing other duties as directed by the talent board.

The talent program shall annually report to the board on the talent program's operations and recommendations, including the results of the apprenticeship pilot program described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105 Computer science education master plan.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
The talent board, in consultation with the state board and the talent program, shall develop a computer science education master plan that:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(1): includes a statement of the objectives and goals of the master plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(2): 53B-34-106 describes how the talent board and the state board will administer the Computer Science for Utah Grant Program created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(3): provides guidance for local education agencies in implementing computer science education opportunities for students in high school, middle school, and elementary school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(4): integrates recommendations and best practices from private and public entities that are seeking to improve and expand the opportunities for computer science education, including the Expanding Computer Education Pathways Alliance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5): 53B-34-106(6) makes recommendations to assist a local education agency in creating a local education agency computer science plan described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5)(a): providing recommendations regarding course offerings in computer science;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5)(b): providing recommendations regarding professional development opportunities in computer science for licensed teachers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5)(c): providing recommendations regarding curriculum software for computer science courses;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5)(d): providing recommendations regarding assessment solutions to measure the learning outcomes of students in computer science courses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-105(5)(e): providing information regarding how a local education agency can receive technical support from the talent board in providing computer science education opportunities for students.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107 Apprenticeships and work-based learning.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(1): The talent program, in collaboration with the talent board, may partner with one or more of the following to facilitate and encourage apprenticeship opportunities and work-based learning opportunities for Utah students:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(1)(a): the State Board of Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(1)(b): the Utah system of higher education; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(1)(c): a participating employer in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(2): Subject to appropriations from the Legislature and in accordance with the proposal process and other provisions of this section, the talent board, in coordination with the talent program, may provide funding for approved apprenticeship opportunities and work-based learning opportunities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3): (1); 53B-16-102 To receive funding under this section, an entity described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a): 53B-16-102 the proposal shall include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(i): a description of the proposed apprenticeship program or work-based learning program that demonstrates the program will be:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(i)(A): responsive to the workforce needs of a high demand industry or occupation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(i)(B): a partnership between at least one participating employer and at least one public high school, technical college, or institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(ii): an estimate of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(ii)(A): student enrollment in the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(ii)(B): what school credit, credentials, certifications, or other workforce attainments will be provided by the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(ii)(C): job-placement rates for students who complete the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(iii): a description of any financial contributions or in-kind contributions that will be provided by each participating employer in the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(iv): 53B-16-102 if the program would require state board approval under the provisions of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(a)(v): the amount of funding requested for the program, including justification for the funding; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b): while not required, a preference may be given to a proposal that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b)(i): a description of a stackable credentialing pathway for participating students that will be created by the program between at least two of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b)(i)(A): a public high school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b)(i)(B): a technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b)(i)(C): an institution of higher education; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(3)(b)(ii): the potential for participating students to obtain full-time employment with the participating employer upon completion of the program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(4): (3)(a); (3)(b) The talent board shall review and prioritize each proposal received and determine whether the proposal should be funded, using the following criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(4)(a): (3)(a) the quality and completeness of the elements of the proposal described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(4)(b): (3)(b) the quality of the optional elements of the proposal described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(4)(c): to what extent the proposal would expand the capacity to meet state or regional workforce needs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(4)(d): other relevant criteria as determined by the talent board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5): (5)(d) A partnership that receives funding under this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(a): shall use the money to accomplish the proposed apprenticeship program or work-based learning program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(b): may use the money to offset a participating employer's direct operational costs associated with employing students as part of an approved apprenticeship program or work-based learning program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(c): (5)(d) except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(d): may use the money to support one full-time employee within a career and technical education region if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(d)(i): each participating local education agency, public high school, technical college, and institution of higher education agree on which entity will house the full-time employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(d)(ii): the full-time employee spends all of the employee's time working exclusively to develop apprentice programs or work-based learning programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(5)(d)(iii): the full-time employee is responsible for regular reporting to and receiving training from the director of the talent program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6): 53B-34-104 The talent program shall be responsible for the administration of apprenticeship programs and work-based learning programs described in this section, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(a): working with and providing technical assistance to the participating partners that establish apprentice programs and work-based learning programs and that receive funding under the provisions of this section;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(b): establishing reporting requirements for participating partners that establish apprentice programs and work-based learning programs and that receive funding under the provisions of this section;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(c): providing outreach and marketing to encourage more employers to participate; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(d): 53B-34-104 annually reporting on the activities, successes, and challenges of the talent program related to administering apprentice programs and work-based learning programs for inclusion in the report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(d)(i): specific entities that received funding under this section;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(d)(ii): the amount of funding provided to each entity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(6)(d)(iii): the number of participating students in each apprentice program and work-based learning program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(7): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-107(7)(a): the method and deadlines for applying for funding under this section;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108 Utah Works Program.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(1): There is created the Utah Works Program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(2): The Utah Works Program, under the direction of the talent board, shall partner with the following entities to develop short-term pre-employment training and short-term early employment training for student and workforce participants that meet the needs of businesses that are creating jobs and economic growth in the state:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(2)(a): the Department of Workforce Services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(2)(b): the Governor's Office of Economic Opportunity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(2)(c): businesses that have significant hiring demands for primarily newly created jobs in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(3): (2) In addition to the duties described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(3)(a): coordinate with the Department of Workforce Services, education agencies, and employers to create effective recruitment initiatives to attract student and workforce participants and business participants to the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(3)(b): coordinate with the board to develop educational and training resources to provide student participants in the program qualifications to be hired by business participants in the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(3)(c): coordinate with the state board and local education agencies when appropriate to develop educational and training resources to provide student participants in the program qualifications to be hired by business participants in the program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(4): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The board, in consultation with the talent board, may, in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(5): The Utah Works Program shall annually report the following metrics to the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(5)(a): the number of participants in the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(5)(b): how program participants learned about or were referred to the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(5)(c): the number of participants who have completed training offered by the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-108(5)(d): the number of participants who have been hired by a business participating in the program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109 Grants for business entities offering employee return to work programs.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(1): As used in this section, "business entity" means a for-profit or nonprofit entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(2): Subject to appropriations from the Legislature, the talent program, in consultation with the talent board, may award grants to business entities to offer innovative return to work programs for employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(3): A business entity that receives grant funds under this section may only use grant funds for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(3)(a): costs associated with developing a new return to work program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(3)(b): costs associated with expanding an existing return to work program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(4): 53B-34-104 The talent program shall include the following information in the report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(4)(a): the process by which the talent program determines which business entities shall receive grants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(4)(b): the formula for awarding grants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-34-109(5): The talent program shall award grant funds on a rolling basis, until the earlier of funds being exhausted or June 30, 2025.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 35 - Higher Education and Corrections Council
***************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "council" means the Higher Education and Corrections Council created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201 Higher Education and Corrections Council.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(1): There is created the Higher Education and Corrections Council to advise the board, the Education Interim Committee, and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee regarding the development and delivery of accredited higher education curriculum to incarcerated individuals in the state correctional system.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2): The council consists of the following 11 members:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(a): a member of the House of Representatives whom the speaker of the House of Representatives appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(b): a member of the Senate whom the president of the Senate appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(c): the commissioner or the commissioner's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(d): the following two members whom the commissioner appoints and who are engaged in prison education and have expertise in transfer articulation:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(d)(i): one employee of a technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(d)(ii): one employee of a degree-granting institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(e): the following two members whom the governor appoints:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(e)(i): an individual who actively researches higher education delivered in a corrections setting using evidence-based practices; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(e)(ii): a formerly incarcerated individual who participated in postsecondary educational programs while incarcerated;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(f): one member of the Board of Pardons and Parole whom the chair of the Board of Pardons and Parole appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(g): the executive director of the Department of Corrections or the executive director's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(h): one employee of the Department of Corrections with expertise in education whom the executive director of the Department of Corrections appoints; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(2)(i): the executive director of the Department of Workforce Services or the executive director's designee.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(a): 36-2-2; Title 5, Chapter 3, Legislator Compensation The salary and expenses of a council member who is a legislator shall be paid in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(b): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A council member who is not a legislator:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(b)(i): may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service on the council; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(b)(ii): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 may receive per diem and reimbursement for travel expenses that the council member incurs as a council member at the rates that the Division of Finance establishes under:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(b)(ii)(A): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(4)(b)(ii)(B): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 rules that the Division of Finance makes under Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(5)(a): A majority of the council members constitutes a quorum.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(5)(b): The action of a majority of a quorum constitutes an action of the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-201(6): The commissioner shall provide staff support to the council.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202 Council duties -- Reporting.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1): The council shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(a): coordinate, facilitate, and support the delivery of higher education in the state's correctional facilities to prepare incarcerated individuals for integration and productive employment upon release;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b): explore and provide recommendations to the board and the Utah Department of Corrections for the efficient and effective delivery of higher education programs to incarcerated individuals, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(i): evidence-based practices and technologies;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(ii): methods of maximizing and facilitating incarcerated individuals' access to educational programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iii): methods of supporting and facilitating timely completion of courses, certificates, and degrees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv): methods of emphasizing educational programs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(A): align with current and future workforce demands of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(B): lead to occupations that are accessible to released incarcerated individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(C): provide sustainable wages following release; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(D): maximize accessibility and timely completion during incarceration;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(v): use of cross-institutional application of coursework toward certificates and degrees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(vi): use of coursework that encourages personal and civic development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(vii): methods of leveraging innovative course delivery, including technology resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c): explore methods and make recommendations for the collection and analysis of critical data regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(i): enrollment and completion of postsecondary education courses, certificate programs, credentials, and degree programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(ii): federal and state student aid awarded to incarcerated individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(iii): costs of postsecondary education in prison, including any recommendations for continued improvement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(iv): outcomes of formerly incarcerated individuals who participated in postsecondary programming during incarceration if the individual is under the supervision of the Department of Corrections, including recidivism, employment, and post-release postsecondary education engagement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(d): recommend requests for legislative appropriations to the board to support the purposes and objectives of the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2): The council shall annually report regarding the council's plans and programs, the number of enrollees served, and the number of enrollees receiving degrees and certificates to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(a): the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(b): before the committee's November interim committee meeting, the Education Interim Committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(c): at least 30 days before the beginning of the annual legislative session, the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 36 - Southern Utah University
***********************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-36-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-36-201 Helen Foster Snow Cultural Center.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Subject to legislative appropriations, Southern Utah University shall establish the Helen Foster Snow Cultural Center to provide language support and cultural opportunities to students studying the Mandarin Chinese language.
